Mr. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon Jo

1)
Points of Caution for Believers
If a person represents ten people, he becomes like a parent to them. When standing in such a position, he must take full responsibility for all the difficulties of those ten people and care for all of them. 
The most dangerous thing in faith life is when one is in such a position; if even one person is in difficulty or lacking, one feels a sense of responsibility to comfort and guide that person. 
However, if the ten people are in a position where they say, "I am in a position of being dragged along. You are higher than me, the 36 families, 72 families, 124 families, 430 families, so you must set an example for me in every way, guide me, and provide for me," then that position is always one where complaints and dissatisfaction can arise. 
Whether eating, working, or sleeping, if one acts centered on oneself and always hopes for personal gain from the results, even if living among ten people, if all ten are in such a mindset, it is easy to become adversarial. 
However, when living centered on the ten people and standing in the position of representing them, the difficulties of the ten become one's own difficulties. 
Thus, if one thinks, "Complaining about the person next to me is the same as complaining about myself. I am in a position of cursing myself," then even if feelings of dissatisfaction arise, they will be the last to manifest. 
The most dangerous thing on the path of faith is complaining and dissatisfaction. Where there is complaining and dissatisfaction, there is no progress or fulfillment. Therefore, what does Satan always target in our believers? What does Satan always present as a weapon before us? It is complaining and dissatisfaction. 
So, what kind of place is a place of complaining and dissatisfaction? It is a place where one reveals their individuality centered on themselves. For example, if there are ten people, the person who always has the notion of self will complain if the other nine do not harmonize and move together. 
You must understand that Satan always establishes itself in places of complaining and dissatisfaction. The best way to remove Satan is to block the path of complaining and dissatisfaction. When dissatisfaction arises, no matter how well one believed in the past, if one becomes dissatisfied, they will become half-hearted. This means believing half and doubting half. This does not mean that the standard of faith rises; rather, since one believes half and doubts half, the foundation becomes half as narrow. Being half-hearted means being halved. What one used to believe fully becomes diminished by half when one becomes half-hearted. 
To be halved means to be distanced by the same amount as one. What one used to believe fully becomes distanced from God by that much when one becomes half-hearted. As one distances from God, Satan comes in and occupies that space. When one complains and is dissatisfied, what does it bring to them? It inevitably brings a half-hearted mindset. 
In your family life, if a wife complains about her husband, she will think, "Why would my husband love me? He doesn’t love me." This half-heartedness inevitably intervenes. When such half-heartedness arises, what happens? The standards she used to have regarding her husband, or the love she used to feel, all diminish. 
When half-heartedness reaches a peak, what happens? Rebellion, conflict, and division arise. At first, there is rebellion, and when rebellion occurs, then fighting begins. If there is rebellion here, there will be rebellion there as well, and when they clash two or three times, fighting ensues. When fighting occurs, everyone suffers. It leads to division. One side must inevitably be lost. 
When one side is lost, who is it? It is the one who first complained, who was half-hearted, who rebelled, and who initiated the fight. You must understand this. Also, who else suffers? The one who first created such motives suffers. 
When one is idle but complains, when there is nothing particularly wrong but one is half-hearted and rebellious, there will inevitably be a resolution. One of the two will be lost, and the other will win. Then the question arises: who loses and who wins? What is right and what is wrong? These become issues. Here, there will inevitably be a struggle between good and evil. Evil first becomes the motive to start complaining and dissatisfaction, and those who complain and are half-hearted will inevitably be removed. You must understand this. In living centered on ten people, those who unnecessarily get annoyed, complain, and criticize will ultimately have to retreat from the group of ten. 
Therefore, what is the most frightening thing in faith life? It is having complaints and dissatisfaction towards God. It is being half-hearted towards God. Not only being half-hearted but also opening one’s mouth to rebel against God. When one rebels, there will inevitably be conflict. Satan targets such places. Satan's strategy is to use such situations to bring down one person. Therefore, if one goes through such a process, they will inevitably be broken. 
So, what should believers especially be cautious about? They should not get caught up in difficult environments. Therefore, do not be half-hearted, do not complain, and do not rebel. This is the most necessary weapon in capturing Satan and exterminating him. What are the weapons that welcome Satan and allow him to win? It is complaining, dissatisfaction, half-heartedness, rebellion, and conflict. You must understand this. 
To be a person with whom God can be present, 
we must stand in the opposite position. To stand in the opposite position, what must we do? If there are ten people, we must take responsibility on behalf of the ten. We must stand in the position of living for the whole ten, and because of the whole ten. 
A person in such a position will help resolve the complaints of others when there are those who complain. Whose work is it to resolve? It is God's work. This is how it works. Leading the wicked who disturb the environment onto a good path is something God must fight and prepare for, but a person who represents the ten takes it upon themselves to resolve the disturbances in that environment. 
To resolve, embrace, and support others is their own work, but because they are doing God's work, they remain. Do you understand what I mean? They remain because they stand in the position of doing God's work. 
When those who complain see someone sacrificing themselves for the whole, they will feel ashamed of their complaints. This is how it works. They will come to know all the sacrifices made day and night for them. That person has such achievements, but they have none, so they feel ashamed of their complaints. Thus, they may start to complain but will feel ashamed and withdraw. 
Even if one sacrifices themselves for the whole, they are like a shield defending against evil on behalf of God, even if their body is on the ground. Therefore, God cannot help but be with such a person. Thus, those who fight against this person will be defeated. You must understand this. 
So how can one work on behalf of God? One must have the mindset that they are taking responsibility on behalf of the whole. One must have the mindset of representing the whole. When there is a hindrance before the whole, one must recognize it as their responsibility and pray with all their heart, even staying up all night. A person in such a position, even if their body is on the ground, is in a position to carry out God's work, and therefore God cooperates with them. 
Thus, in that position, one cannot help but develop. There, joy, glory, and hope remain, and strong power resides. God is with them. Because God is with them, life force is infused. There, the heart of love continues. 
What is the first step to becoming such a person? One must have the mindset, "I exist for the whole. Therefore, day or night, regardless of the time, I am here for them." Such a person will never fail in the world of Satan. 
However, if one centers on themselves and thinks, "Oh, I didn’t live like this at home. What is this? How can I live eating barley rice? I’ve never eaten barley rice until now. What is this? How can I live in the prayer room every day? How can a woman wear such clothes and go out on the street?" If one has endless complaints like this, 
those of you in the field must fulfill the mission of pioneers, and if you complain, it is endless. If you feel dissatisfaction, it is endless. If you are half-hearted about the purpose, it is endless. If you rebel, it is endless. Because it is endless, it is bad. Therefore, one must not complain or be half-hearted or rebellious, but must absolutely believe and absolutely comply. 
Doing so is to maintain the position of being able to work on behalf of God. The path one takes in this way will inevitably lead to revival and multiplication; this is the principled view. So, what kind of position allows one to carry out God's will in many areas? That position is an extremely difficult one. Isn’t the position that serves the greatest purpose in the most difficult circumstances the one that can do the most of God's work? This is how it is viewed. 
Why are you here as a small woman? You are here for thirty million people, and you are here on behalf of three billion humanity. You are here to remove the conditions of dissatisfaction, half-heartedness, and rebellion of three billion people in the world. 
To be a person who can remain until the end, 
you must absolutely not complain or be dissatisfied. You must also absolutely not be half-hearted. You must believe one hundred percent. Even if you have doubts, you must believe. If you can be deceived once, twice, or three times, that itself will naturally resolve. If you go out with such a mindset, even if you are an individual in such an environment, you are carrying out God's responsibility for the restoration providence at a focal point for the entire world. You must realize that you are in a position of leading responsibility in advancing God's side. You must understand that such a mindset is the most precious position. This is how it becomes. 
Therefore, a person who has the notion that they are in a position for the whole will be the one who can remain until the very end. If they remain until the very end, what happens? If all ten people live and then perish, and that one person remains, they may receive more than their share when the lost resources are gathered. Do you understand what I mean? If each of the ten people has one million won, then together they have ten million won. If they all go bankrupt with that ten million won, the loss could exceed one million won. 
If the Unification Church goes a certain distance and collapses, how can one be the person who does not perish? They must say that even if the Unification Church collapses and everyone flees, they will remain until the very end, managing everything and organizing it all. If there is someone with such thoughts, even if the Unification Church ends, God can use that person for a different purpose later on. Such a person can find a new path to be guided. 
Therefore, the Bible says, "The one who endures to the end will be saved." It is not about standing in the middle. It is not about giving up halfway. Is it the end when two people remain? Even if one is left alone, they must endure until the end. Until death, do not complain, do not be half-hearted, do not rebel, and endure. 
Even Jesus said until the end, "Abba Father, not my will, but yours be done." Jesus' personal will was not for Israel, but the Father's will was for the world, so he did so until death. Before the will for the world, one's own will must be guided. If the will for the world is left, then my will will be revived. Therefore, Jesus stood in a position of denying himself, saying he would go centered on the Father's will. Thus, although Jesus died, it seemed like he perished, he actually thrived. Why? Because God was with him. Those who die in such a way will be resurrected. When we look at historical saints and sages, those who die in such a way will surely be exalted in later generations. This is how it becomes. 
You must overcome reality and fight on behalf of God. 
What is the work you do for God? Going out to evangelize is not the work done for God. First, you must know how to live on behalf of the ten people to spread God's work widely in the world. You must become a responsible person who can fully take responsibility for the family and on behalf of the ten people so that you can face a hundred people wherever you go. If you are in a position of leading nine people while being responsible for ten, then you are not qualified. In such a position, how can you save eleven people? You cannot save them. 
In such a position, there are countless conditions for complaining, dissatisfaction, half-heartedness, and rebellion.
14   Points of Caution for Believers

It is a matter of concern. Moreover, there are plenty of such conditions for those who are currently out as members of the Unification Church. The mother-in-law and father-in-law are scolding, and the brother-in-law and sister-in-law, without exception, all oppose. Furthermore, there are complaints at home as well. The husband and children are complaining, asking, "What is this?" They are sitting right on top of a pile of complaints. It is perfectly suited for dissatisfaction, perfectly suited for complaints, perfectly suited for doubt, and perfectly suited for rebellion. Is that right or not? It would not be strange at all if there were more opposition, dissatisfaction, and doubt.

When Jesus died, he was alone and a bachelor. However, when you die, it is not just you; it is as if your husband and children die with you, which means you are a pile of complaints. Therefore, if you want to doubt, there is no end to it. Complaining, "What does this mean?" has no end. Isn't that right? If you start to doubt, thinking, "Is the teacher using us for his own gain?" there is no end to that either. Once you start to doubt in a chain reaction, is there an end or not? There is no end. There is no end to it.

Next, you will surely think, "I joined the Unification Church for no reason. When I was in college, I was praised by my teachers as an excellent student, but now I am being pointed at and whispered about everywhere I go. How can I live like this?" This is perfectly suited for complaints and dissatisfaction.

The fact that such complaints remain is true. Then think about whether this is the ultimate station or final destination for complaints on this earth. When you think about the place where you are currently evangelizing, is it the last place in the human world where you can complain? There may be even worse places than this.

To restore, you must achieve complete restoration. Therefore, you must go to the place where you can complain the most and return victorious without complaining. Otherwise, you will not be able to achieve complete restoration. When you think about it this way, you are standing in a place where you cannot yet achieve complete restoration. This is how the teacher thinks.

Restoration through indemnity means turning things around. To restore through indemnity, what was turning left must turn right. It must turn around. It must turn around and create another world.

So, when your heart is filled with complaints and dissatisfaction, will heaven be in the midst of that, or not? Will heaven have any room to enter that heart, or not? Heaven does not exist where there are complaints and dissatisfaction. Heaven moves far away from places of complaints and dissatisfaction. Then, if you are doubting and rebelling, it completely departs. A place of complaints, dissatisfaction, doubt, and rebellion always becomes the lair of Satan.

Therefore, you must center on God's will and create God's front line. If you have a heart of complaints, dissatisfaction, doubt, and rebellion, you must suppress that heart and say, "I am a representative of God. Even if everything fails, I will not fail. I will hold on to what is failing and not let it fail." A person with such a heart cannot be loved by God more than anyone else in that era, in that place, and in that environment. Do you understand? That is how it becomes. Therefore, the place where he stands is a place of fighting on behalf of God. It is a place of fighting for God's will.

How to Turn Satan's Things into God's

In your evangelism, you must first evangelize ten people. Do you understand? When you evangelize, each of you must evangelize ten people first. To evangelize, do you have to sacrifice or not? You must sacrifice. If you do that, God will surely help you. By doing so, God helps from the opposite side.

However, if you evangelize while complaining and being dissatisfied, will you be able to evangelize? If there are ten people and you are complaining, "What is the purpose of this?" will those people listen to you? Will they listen or not? No matter how much you praise them and ask them to listen to you, if you are complaining, evangelism will absolutely not happen.

So what should you do? You must endure and sacrifice, so you cannot complain. There is no other way than to endure and sacrifice. Isn't that right? If you endure and sacrifice, will ten people think badly of me? "They will think well of you." You know that, right? Will the whole group support me or undermine me? They will support you. If you cannot endure and overcome, they may stop supporting you. However, if you continue to endure and overcome, they will continue to support you. Therefore, you must endure to the end. You must be patient and overcome. You must endure.

In serving God, the very first step is to endure and bear. Who do you endure for? You must endure for the whole. You must have a central thought for the purpose of the whole and endure until it is achieved. There can be no complaints and dissatisfaction in that. By doing so, the heavenly kingdom and the foundation of heaven expand.

God is always the center of the universe and the one responsible for the whole, so it is more precious than anything to have the belief that I also represent the center of the whole. You must surely understand this. Do you understand? You must say that you are for the whole. If you say you are for yourself, you will fail. This can lead to a multitude of complaints and dissatisfaction.

However, when you represent thirty million people, how many people among those thirty million are more miserable than you? Are there not people dying even at this moment? Are there not people groaning in pain on their sickbeds at this moment? Are there not many who wish to freely stroll in the yard and freely climb the mountains but cannot? Are there not people who want to express their stories to someone but are groaning in misery because they cannot? Thinking of these things, you must say, "I am a sacrifice to indemnify all these complaints and dissatisfaction, so I will gladly accept even more complaints."

Saying that you will gladly accept complaints does not mean you want to become rich in complaints. If you accept complaints, you should become rich in complaints, but instead, you will become rich in heaven. So how do you become rich in heaven? You must take away what belongs to the world of Satan. Then, the wealth that comes from taking away from the world of Satan will increase proportionally.

When I say I will bear all the conditions of human complaints, doubts, and all rebellion, does that mean I will become the representative of complaints and dissatisfaction? Does it mean I will become the representative of doubt and rebellion? I will take it upon myself and subdue it. This mindset is the most urgent in faith life.

When the authority of national complaints, the authority of doubt, or the authority of rebellion bows down and obeys, then indemnity begins. Who causes that to happen? It begins with myself, so I become a person who works on behalf of God in that nation. Therefore, I will naturally receive blessings for the nation. Receiving blessings takes a little time. Since it takes time, you must wait until the end. You must endure until the entire nation surrenders. You must endure and bear.

God's Strategy to Lead the Good Side

When any district leader or head of the Unification Church says, "I have endured and borne for over 15, 17, or 20 years, so that should be enough. I can't endure anymore," will that work? Even if the teacher says he cannot endure anymore and retreats, will the Unification Church collapse because that person says so? If the teacher persistently endures and perseveres, it will not collapse. Moreover, when a person who is complaining sees the teacher, do they feel dignified? They feel ashamed in front of someone who stands in the central position and takes responsibility. You must understand that this is the secret of indemnity in the ongoing battle between good and evil.

Therefore, wherever you go, if you cannot do that, it becomes a big problem. Complaining is a condition that Satan likes. To eliminate this, you must fight, saying, "Let’s see what you can do." When you go out to evangelize, the neighborhood will make a fuss, curse, oppose, and persecute you. At that time, it is better to have allies around you than to be alone. When ten people are together, even if they quarrel, when persecution comes from the world of Satan, they will think, "Oh, this is not good." At that time, they will want to unite.

Therefore, even if they were not united among themselves, when a great battle with the enemy breaks out, they will become one. If someone goes out and causes a problem, and the neighborhood makes a fuss, a greater Satan will appear and act. When the neighbors see that the conscientious person is being persecuted by wicked people, they will side with the conscientious person. It is the same. Even if they are in a position to be on the side of Satan, if a more wicked villain appears and creates a fuss, they will want to side with the good side. Such a principled action can gather people together.

For example, if a mother and father in a household have been fighting since dawn, and the angry wife curses her husband as he goes out, saying, "That man, may he die today," and then, sure enough, the husband goes out and gets into an accident and dies, what will that wife do? "Oh no, I was wrong." When a major incident occurs, she will say, "Oh, I was wrong. Please forgive me."

That is why God carries out this strategy. If there is no one who can take responsibility in any position, He allows even more wicked groups to come in. By allowing them to come in, He makes them unite. This is the strategy He employs. The Israelites were also attacked because they could not believe in God well. That is the method. Do you understand?

Therefore, external persecution is not a bad thing. When you become completely united, there will be no persecution. Even if a mob of ten comes to attack our house, if the eight family members hold onto each other tightly, they cannot be dragged away. If they become fierce like this, they cannot make a fuss.

If you take responsibility and fight with ten people, there will be no external persecution. Do you understand? When you go out united, there will be no external persecution, but when you are not united and retreat, more wicked groups will come with clubs to beat you. At that time, you will say, "Oh no, this is not good. God!" and you will unite. Therefore, it is a principle that each person must unite from the position of representing ten people to prevent such things from happening.

From this standpoint, when you have the heart to devour all conditions of complaints, dissatisfaction, doubt, and rebellion, and you go out with patience and responsibility for the whole, when those ten people succeed because of you, you will always be in the position of a mother to those ten people. Then they will say, "Oh, where are you going, mother? I want to follow you." Will that happen or not? It will happen.

When someone who is like a mother, an older brother, or the closest friend talks about the heavenly kingdom, it will taste good, but when someone else talks, it will feel unpleasant. Will you become a person who is delightful or a person who is utterly unpleasant? What kind of person will you be? You must become someone everyone likes, right? "Yes."

You must walk the path of indemnity with the heart of a parent.

Since you represent thirty million people and the entire human race, you must respond to the conditions of complaints, doubts, rebellion, and struggles that arise in that context, and God can create such environments to indemnify our ten family members.

At that time, who will take responsibility? When someone gladly accepts that and struggles, claiming it as their own responsibility, the external world of Satan begins to crumble. This is how the history of indemnity unfolds. Do you understand?

That is why you must have the heart of a parent. You must have the heart of a parent who is the master. Therefore, you must say, "With the heart of a parent, I will use the body of a servant, my sweat for the earth, my tears for humanity, and my blood for heaven." Only on such days can you not be a substitute for a parent. If a parent complains, what should the children do? Children who think, "Oh no, this is a big deal," must die. If a parent cries, the children must be willing to die for their parents. You must understand that. That is why such a slogan has been established.

This is a thought that unifies around a subjective idea. It is a unifying thought centered on the subject. Then what does the "통" in "통일" mean? It means "to lead" (統). The position of leading means to serve. It means to guide. How hard is it to lead everyone? By leading everyone, when they finally reach a comfortable position, then they will want to serve. At that time, since it is comfortable and there is nothing to complain about, they will say, "Ah, how good is this because of whom? Because of the teacher," and they will serve gratefully even if they are not asked to.

Therefore, until the time of glory when all people can serve, you must always bear that responsibility, and you cannot escape the path of suffering.

The One Who Will Receive the Greatest Reward at the End

Today, when looking at the Unification Church centered on the teacher, in Daegu or any district, when something happens, the teacher suffers more than the district leaders. You worry, but your worries do not end there. In the Unification Church, if you make a mistake, all the responsibility falls on the teacher. Other organizations do not do that, but in our Unification Church, even a small incident leads people to say, "Oh, look at the Unification Church. What is Teacher Moon doing?" and they blame everything on the teacher.

Is it bad to take on responsibility, or is it good? "It is good." Taking on responsibility is good. It is not bad to take it on; it is good. (Laughter)

Until now, religious organizations in South Korea have all blamed the teacher. Is that good or bad? It is good. Among the people of South Korea, if someone is struggling because they cannot get married, we Unification Church members are willing to take that on wholesale. Is that good or bad? So, in what position do we take it on? We must take it on not with our husbands but by losing our husbands. We must take it on not with our children but by losing our children. We must take it on not with our siblings and relatives but by losing them all.

If we take it on after losing everything, when it comes time to give rewards, who should receive them first? Answer me. Should it be given to those who have, or to those who do not have? It should be given to those who do not have. Is someone who does not have a person of resentment or a person of love? If it is a person of love, when God wants to give rewards, should He give the worst or the best? "The best." He gives the best. Therefore, the one who has taken on difficulties receives the good reward. Since they have worked from a position of having lost everything, when it comes time to give rewards, they should be given even better ones.

Thus, they become the best husbands among husbands. They become the best children among children.
The superior parent among parents, the superior relative among relatives, the superior nation among nations, the superior world among worlds, 
becoming the superior master among masters. This is possible. Thinking this way makes me feel good, doesn’t it? “Yes, it feels good.” How good does it feel? It feels wonderfully good.

So, is this about dying or living? “It’s about living.” Is it about receiving blessings or being ruined? “It’s about receiving blessings.” Not only receiving blessings but also bringing in the blessings that already exist. It’s about attracting them. It’s about gathering them. Who gathers those blessings? It is God who gathers them. Because of this, many spiritual mediums who connect with the spiritual world all say that when they see the spiritual world, they cling to the teacher.

Everyone, now you know the secret to receiving rewards, right? If you have received such rewards, are they wonderful rewards or trivial ones? “They are wonderful rewards.” What kind of reward do you want to exchange it for, a reward that cannot be exchanged? It cannot be exchanged, so it is the happiest thing. You need to understand that. Today, we are the only ones who focus on this method for the sake of our nation and the world. Look around you. Which organization today does such work?

Looking at today, the end times are almost here, right? When the end times come, if any person or religious organization claims to work for God just like us, should they receive better rewards or worse rewards than us? “They should receive better rewards.” They should receive better rewards. Then do you want to receive better rewards than those people or worse rewards? “I want to receive better rewards.”

If you want to receive better rewards, should you stand in front or behind? “You should stand in front.” If a prize is given to the person who eats the most, they must eat more than others. If a prize is given to the person who dresses well, they must wear the best clothes. Conversely, if you want to be the best at not eating and enduring, you must endure the least. Doesn’t that feel unpleasant? Does it feel unpleasant or good?

Therefore, even if the Unification Church is at the brink of being worn out and bent, we must say, “We work for something greater than anyone else. We work for the world.” Even if we die, we must die that way. Where is there an organization that has died like that?

If God quietly calculates and finds that the degree has reached 99 degrees, and only one degree is needed to reach 100 degrees, would He feel good or bad looking at that 99 degrees? That one degree is more precious than 99 degrees. Do you like 100 points or 99 points? Can you exchange a thousand 99-point scores for one 100-point score? Raise your hand if you think that’s possible. Doesn’t God have such circumstances as well? Right? Ultimately, where is the place that can be restored to 100 points? Have you thought about that? There must be such a place.

The place where you can receive the highest reward
Now our Unification organization is moving for the sake of the entire world. In fulfilling God’s will, if we endure and persevere, God’s will will inevitably be accomplished. Right? Even if I don’t say it, doesn’t the world say, “If you endure and persevere, you will be blessed?” When we unite, we live, and when we scatter? “We die.” You know that. You know it, but because you can’t do it, you perish. If you could do that, you wouldn’t perish.

Where is the standard of 100 points in enduring and persevering? The standard is to lay down your life. If you lay down your life and die, your parents will cry out, “Why are you dying? Live a little longer!” and your siblings will say, “Oh, brother, sister, why are you dying now?” Your whole family will be in an uproar. Therefore, you must be in a position of solitude. Even if you are alone, it’s not about going out to play and dying, but being in a place where the enemy is trying to kill you, where a group of ten is trying to kill you, where a nation is moving and the world is moving to try to kill you. If you can be in such a place for God, then God will bless that place. Right?

So, the Unification Church should not only be opposed by South Korea, Japan, and the United States but should be opposed by the whole world. If that happens, do you like it or not? “I like it.” It sounds good in words, but try experiencing it. What will your eyes look like, and how will your face look? You haven’t experienced it, have you? You must go through such things. Even if you are pushed, you must say, “I will take responsibility and defend for God, and I will fight for God. As long as God exists, I will never be uprooted. I will never perish.”

Why won’t you perish? Because if my life, which fights for God, is targeted, the enemy will be punished for three generations. If more than three generations are broken, more than three generations will arise. Therefore, when the opposing side moves to attack and then retreats, I will gain that much benefit. Three practical methods for restoration and recovery
God has sacrificed what is closest to Him until now, loving the wicked Cain more than His own sons and daughters. Therefore, we must go through such a position. What does patience and overcoming mean? It means to endure and persevere. Is there anyone who likes to endure and persevere? Raise your hand if you do. There’s not a single one. There is an old story. In a certain family where five generations lived together, there was a grandmother who lived as a daughter-in-law. To capture and destroy God’s enemies and the enemies of humanity, we must risk our lives to completely surround and annihilate the enemy. Next, it’s not enough to just endure and persevere. If you endure and persevere while saying, “Oh, this is hard!” will that do? The one who gives and forgets is the blessed one.

It would be better not to give at all. Do you understand?

For this reason, giving one-third is worse than not giving at all. If you are going to give, you must give two-thirds. This is because the fall occurred during the restoration and growth stages, which were at the two-thirds level. Anything above the two-thirds level is the completion level and can belong to heaven. Therefore, those who give beyond the two-thirds standard can enter the kingdom of heaven. To meet the two-thirds standard, you cannot just have 50% or 60%. Since three times three is nine, you must exceed 60% and reach 70%.

Even when you are in school taking exams and receiving scores, there is only a 10-point difference between 60 and 70, yet receiving a 70 feels better. From a score of 7, all hopes begin to spread. After going through six days, when the Sabbath arrives, hope begins to sprout. People say it is good to have a score of 70. You cannot fail the association principle exam if you do not score at least 70. If you do not score 70, you fail. You must exceed 70 to pass. That is how it has been decided.

For this reason, you must have a heart that gives more than two-thirds. However, if you think, "I gave this much yesterday, so I should get that much back. That is a merchant. Such a person is not a parent. You must give two-thirds and forget the thought that you gave. Those who help others and remember their help cannot receive blessings quickly. The believer's caution
If someone records in a notebook how much they helped others and thinks, "Since I helped, I should expect help in return," that person will not receive the blessings of their contributions. You must always have the same heart when giving as you do when you receive. Even if you have helped many, if you forget that and do not recognize your help, blessings are already in front of you. "How long has it been that you forgot?" This is the situation. Do you understand? This applies to thousands of years and even tens of thousands of years. Just as forgetting after tens of thousands of years is the same.

For this reason, those who help others and forget will receive blessings quickly. Those who think, "I helped, so they should repay me," will not receive blessings no matter how long they wait. Do you understand? If you only think about receiving and not about giving, then such people are all Satan. God does not come out in that. If you only like receiving, God will not help you.

If I say I will give you something, everyone will scramble to get something good. In that case, one will go to heaven and the other will go to hell. For this reason, actions for oneself should be slow, and actions for others should be hurried. This is the teaching of the sages. So, is it good or bad to hastily prepare for the work for others without being ready? It is good. Do you understand? The conditions of disbelief overcome by love
Jesus faced opposition from the nation and the church while walking the path of His will, and furthermore, He was beaten by His relatives and even abandoned by His beloved disciples. How shocked must Jesus have been at this? You must understand this.

When a beloved child says to their parents, "How can you be my mom and dad?" how shocked must the parents feel? Therefore, disbelief on the path of love can become a factor that leads to double destruction. For this reason, we must endure, sacrifice, and be meek and humble. When we consider this position, can we say that Jesus had the right to complain? Jesus is the son sent by God after 4,000 years of preparation to the nation of Israel. That is who Jesus is. Isn't that so? "If you go, the family of Mary and Joseph will unite, and Judaism and the nation of Israel will welcome you as their king." This was God's promise. But what is this? He was labeled a murderer, a robber, and a rebel, and was accused of trying to overthrow the sovereignty of the nation. It did not match at home, nor did it match in the nation. Furthermore, God did not say, "Endure," but left Jesus to fend for Himself.

So, did Jesus feel deceived? Did He feel cheated? Did it seem like things were going according to the promise? Everything went wrong. So, His heart must have been filled with dissatisfaction. He can rebel. Even in such a position, Jesus went forward.

Good deeds are good deeds until the end. Coming for the nation is a good thing. Coming to represent the church is being in a good position. The family of the priest Zechariah, centered around John the Baptist, formed a bond with the family of Joseph. They were said to become loyal subjects, so they were good people.

Moreover, Jesus thought that He was opposing from a good position. He believed that He was working for others, not for Himself. He thought that the promised position was certain, and that He Himself was also certain. But why did it not happen? Initially, it was because of Satan, and then it was because of the world of Satan. Therefore, He thought that ignorant people and ignorant church members were being deceived and opposing Him.

If I am a good person whom God recognizes on the final path, then God will answer my prayers." This is what He thought. So, He prayed, "Not my will, but Your will be done." "My will was the promise I made with You, and my death is also a providence of love to save the world, so let Your will be done."

Is there any complaint in that? There is none. Did He say, "If You want, go ahead and do as You please"? He had a heart of gratitude. He offered His body with a heart of gratitude and praise while being in a position of overcoming and enduring. Is that not so? To whom did He offer it? He offered it to God. Jesus felt sorry to present Himself before God, saying, "I cannot offer my death before You. Even if You tell me to die here, I understand that there are paths left for me to die again and again. Since I cannot offer this body before You, please leave it to humanity, my enemy." He died, passing on such feelings to humanity. God, who knows this, cannot help but weep.

This son must not die, so resurrection was realized. True life does not suffer accusations in the world of Satan after death but resurrects as a life that God can support. Such a death opens the path to the kingdom of heaven. Isn't that so?

Please bless us to walk the path of suffering with a heart of compassion for such a nation, and protect us, Father, I earnestly ask.

We thank You for protecting us until now. After spending this remaining day, they will return to all corners of the land, so please guard their lonely steps. They are a group that has taken extraordinary steps to avoid perishing in a perishing world, so let them not become people who shame Your dignity, but let them be a group that can maintain Your honor and receive the blessings of Your eternal and unchanging grace.

Let them become the ancestors that humanity hopes for and the nation that humanity desires, and may they not become a group that betrays Your wishes, Father, I earnestly hope and desire.

Since we have come to know a different path, we find ourselves in this destiny, and because we know Your will, we inevitably find ourselves connected to the fate of sons and daughters. When we think of this, we stand at the crossroads of despair and hopelessness, but we cannot despair.

It is okay for us to perish in despair, but we cannot abandon You or fail to keep Your path because we fear that the people and the world attached to us may perish. Let us be daughters who think this way. Please protect the sons and their children who are worried behind these daughters, and may You protect the blood-related Israel, the external Israel, and the Cain-like foundation, so that this may become the foundation of heavenly victory and the ownership of praise and joy.

I earnestly ask once again that at this time, You make us Your daughters who remain for a long time with Your words, and I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 

2) At the Peak of Suffering
No one in this world likes to work hard. Just as humans do not like difficulties, God does not wish to walk the path of hardship. We know that not only humans but also animals and even plants do not want to be in difficult positions.

However, when we look at the path of restoration centered on God's will today, the path that His will takes is not a path that can avoid suffering. If there were a way for God to avoid the path of suffering, He would have already taken that path. The path of restoration is one that cannot be taken without traversing the path of suffering.

To save fallen humanity, God has worked hard. Since humanity has fallen from its original position, there is no way for humanity to escape from that fallen position. If the only way to escape was to simply go down, that would be one thing, but one cannot trace the path of restoration by simply going down. To walk the path of restoration, one must go back up the path they came.

It is easy to fall. However, to rise again from that fallen position, one must push away all the conditions that were pressed down upon them when they fell. Otherwise, it is impossible to rise.

When we look at an individual, whether it is A or B, that one person has fallen to a level that is equivalent to the deepest valley, the very bottom of the deepest valley. Families press down on individuals, tribes press down on families, nations press down on tribes, and the world presses down on nations. In other words, you must understand that this is the position of fallen humanity today.

Humanity has not fallen alone. While one may have fallen alone, as history has progressed over thousands of years, the burdens have increased and become heavier. Therefore, our current position is that of being buried at the very bottom of a pit or valley. We must understand that this is the state of humanity.

For humanity to be revived and to meet the foundation and time of hope again, it cannot remain in its current position. There is no way to escape from here. If humanity could find an easy and free path to recovery from the position they have fallen into, how much would God desire that path and how much would He want them to walk it? However, because of the fall, humanity is in a state of being crushed in the valley of valleys, as depicted in this illustration.

When God says He will save such humanity, we must understand that God's position and our human position are different. For God to save me, He must come down and clear a path because I cannot simply rise on my own. Until He does that, humanity cannot be saved. God must clear a path and come down.

So, what path has God walked to unfold the providential will centered on me? Conversely, He has worked through history, breaking through the world, the nation, the people, the tribes, and families to reach me.

Today’s Position
Today, if you have been called to the position of the will for 5 years, 10 years, or even 20 years, you must understand that the path you have followed to know the will and follow God began only 5, 10, or 20 years ago. However, when you think about the historical background, you must realize that God has worked for thousands of years to bridge the gap for one person—me.

To save one person, God has removed the Satan that governs this world, the Satan that blocks this nation and people, and the Satan that obstructs your family. You may not have realized that such efforts have come through a path of suffering and pain that we humans cannot even imagine.
In light of the fact that an entity called 'I' exists before the will, if we compare the cost of the effort God has made with my own value in standing before that will today, my value today is nothing. Even if I stand in a position connected to the will, from the perspective of knowing the will, my value is one that is oppressed by the dominion of death, and I must overcome countless grievances and paths of suffering; I must understand that I have come to know the will in the most difficult position. Although I have come to know the will, it is not from a position of having ascended to this place, but rather from the very bottom. Therefore, when I think about the debt I owe before God's effort as one who knows the will, and when I compare our intrinsic value and our own value with the effort God has made, we must realize that we are in debt that we can never repay before that effort.

We must ascend this path. We must go up as if we are catching a fish. (Writing on the board) This is the path of restoration. When viewed from the center of the individual, it is the way to love individuals. It is all different. Every point of love is not just a continuation of the same path; rather, when the position of love differs and the counterpart of love changes, the history of indemnity emerges, and you must understand this.

When I look at myself from the center of the individual, I am loving myself. However, in order for me, who is loving myself, to enter the path where I can completely receive God's love, my individual self must go through the process of a global battle. For this reason, this position is the farthest away. It is the farthest distance.

The Mission of the Messiah
What has the history of 6,000 years been about? It has been a history aimed at finding one individual. Among individuals, who? It has been a history aimed at finding one man, for whom God has paid the price of effort until now. However, even if one man is found and established, that man is not set at the top of heaven. He is set in this position. Although he stands in this position, it is a place made so that he is not hindered when God comes down. You must understand that the history until now has been about finding one man who stands in a position prepared for that.

If the Lord comes to this earth, in order for the Lord to come to this earth, He must go through the history of indemnity and the history of restoration that began from the day of the fall 6,000 years ago. Thus, at the end of 6,000 years, one man must be found, and that man must be someone who has come down from heaven. When this Lord comes down from heaven, he must appear on a foundation where all conditions of global, national, ethnic, tribal, and clan satanic forces have been cleared away. When that one person appears, he is in a position that has paved the way of indemnity that can go to the world, so it is a principle that Satan cannot accuse or obstruct him in his return. For this reason, you must understand that God has been working hard until now to create a way for that return. Furthermore, you must understand that this central ideology is the ideology of the Messiah.

When the Messiah comes to this earth, he has come after going through the history of indemnity and the path of effort with God's cooperation, but when he returns, he cannot return freely. So how must he return? He must return with his family as an individual. Not only must he return with his family, but he must also bring his tribe. He must not only bring his tribe but also his nation and country; this is the mission of the Messiah that you must understand. Although he came with great effort, he must go without God's cooperation, taking on the responsibility of effort on behalf of God.

Why must it be so? Because of the fall. Who caused that fall? It was not because of God, but because Adam and Eve could not take responsibility and fell. Because of this, the history of 6,000 years has been disrupted, and the Lord who comes in place of Adam must do the work of unraveling this.

The Responsibility of the Bride to Approach the Returning Lord
This work is not done centered on the individual. If it could be done centered on the individual, it would be simple, but the individual does not act alone; he must act as a bride who is called to go out before the Lord who has brought the foundation of historical victory. That bride must also be in alignment with the authority of historical victory.

What does it mean to be a bride standing in the authority of historical victory? It means that the bride must not stand in a position where Satan can accuse her. A bride must be prepared in a position where she cannot be accused by Satan. Thus, the bride and groom must not act freely but must become one. As I mentioned earlier, when Adam and Eve fell, they became fishers. Satan was first, then Eve, then Adam, and all things came last.

Therefore, in ascending, Adam and Eve cannot stand side by side. You must understand this. If Adam and Eve cannot walk side by side, who must lead? The Lord, who is in the position of Adam and must fight against Satan, must lead and take responsibility, while Eve, who is the counterpart, must absolutely obey the Lord and follow in the footsteps of the Lord; otherwise, she cannot be liberated. You must understand this. Thus, the bride and groom must stand in a relationship of front and back, completely united, not in a horizontal or lateral relationship.

Then how must the bride know the Lord, who is the groom? She must know Him as her Father, and then she must know Him as her older brother, and finally as her groom. Adam was created centered on God, and because he is in a position to become the embodiment of God, who will wear the reality in the future, he is in a position of oneness with God, thus being in the position of a father and the position of the oldest brother. Therefore, only after having the relationship to regard Him as a father and as an older brother can she finally establish the relationship of a bride and groom. In other words, Adam was born as the son of God and as the older brother of Eve, so the Lord who comes in this reality has the responsibility to protect the bride on behalf of the Father, and then as an older brother, he must guide the bride, who is in the position of a younger sister. Thus, standing with Eve, who has experienced both parental love and brotherly love, the original principle of creation is that they can finally establish the relationship of bride and groom.

When we consider this, what must the bride, who hopes for the returning Lord, do when He comes? The bride must first establish a heartistic connection with Him as her Father and as her older brother before receiving Him as her groom. This is the principle of restoration that you must understand.

In order for Eve, who stands in the position of the fallen, to receive the Lord as her groom, she must regard Him as her Father and also as her older brother. After going through such a process... Since He is the Father, I must stand in the position of a dutiful daughter, and since He is the older brother, I must follow Him no matter what difficulties arise.

A sibling cannot stand in opposition to the path that the parents take. This applies to both Adam and Eve. Therefore, when Adam goes to the place of death, Eve must also follow that path. When children walk the path of life and death, the parents feel the pain of going to the place of death. When we think about this, centered on heart, the relationship between God and us, or between Jesus and us, is both the relationship of Father and son and the relationship of Father and older brother, which you must understand.

A True Family is the Center of Hope for God and All Creation
Today, we, the descendants of the fallen, have parents of the world. We also have older brothers of the world and husbands of the world. The relationships of parents, siblings, and couples formed within this fallen realm are based on fallen love, and therefore, God cannot relate to them. Thus, what does God demand from fallen humanity today? He demands that we overcome the relationships of fallen bloodline couples, sibling relationships, and parent-child relationships. The question is how to step over and transcend this. It must be done not only in words but also in heart. It must be done not just in words but in reality.

As those in the position of God's children, in the relationship of Father and son with God, we must be above the order of relationships of the world. When considering sibling relationships, we must find a realm that is above the relationships of the world. Also, in the relationship of couples, when we look at the many families that make up the fallen humanity on this earth today, your couple must stand in a position that cannot be compared to the couples of the fallen world. You cannot exchange the couples blessed by God with the couples of the fallen world. Can you exchange the beloved sons and daughters of God with all of humanity in the satanic world? You cannot. 

Can you exchange the beloved son of God with this world? You cannot.

In this way, God cannot say, "This is my son. This is my daughter," or "This is my blessed family," without having created a family that is more precious than any family in the satanic world or any human being in the satanic world. You must understand that without such a family, God cannot stand in a position of dignity and face the world. Why? Because if He is not in such a position, He becomes a God with a family that is worse than Satan, and a God with siblings that are worse than Satan. That cannot be the authority of God.

When we consider the principle of creation, parents must love their children from the highest glorious position, and children must form couples within the realm of God's blessing and become the center of all creation, able to bless and share blessings with all created beings. When we think about this, such a family is the center of the universe, the center of hope that God desires, and the absolute center of hope that all creation longs for.

The fact that such a family could not be established on this earth is precisely the fall. You must understand that the path of restoration is to deny this fallen world and to go toward establishing such a family.

Because this will was to be fulfilled in the Garden of Eden but could not be fulfilled there, we must fulfill it within the realm of the fallen satanic world, and you must understand that it cannot be achieved without laying a foundation through trials thousands of times over.

In other words, the families formed in the world are families formed within the realm of the fallen, so before standing in a position where that family can be received with the joy of having been formed in Eden without falling, God cannot be pleased. You must understand that without presenting such a family, God cannot stand in a position to declare that He will conquer the satanic world today.

From the perspective of God's internal and heartistic position, how difficult and heartbreaking must this position be? You must understand this. It is not that He is happy to bless beloved children; rather, the position of that blessed family is surrounded by the satanic world, facing opposition, accusations, and invasions. Therefore, the heart of God must find a way to love that family as if it were a family formed in the Garden of Eden, where the fallen world has not tasted the realm of fallen love. You must realize how great God's anguish is. Today, we must understand this. Instead of resolving this heartache, we are in a position where we are going through the opposite path of indemnity, which is the position of the Father.

Do you understand the heart of God, who is at the peak of suffering? 

Every time the Father faces that family, He should be joyful, and hope should sprout, and love should be able to flourish, yet they have become children whom He cannot even face. As a Father-son relationship, God should be able to say, "You are bone of my bone, flesh of my flesh," and humans should possess a bond that cannot be severed, but why have they come to stand in the position of enemies?

You must understand that the anguish brought about by the fall is that the Father, who wants to relate with a heart, cannot even think of them as sons. The path to turn back from this fallen position is the path of restoration. However, even if God calls, we are in a position where we cannot look directly toward heaven, and even if we have the freedom to turn toward heaven, we are in a bound position where we cannot go toward heaven. You must understand this.

Originally, what position should humans be in to be called by God? It is not to call humans in this fallen position but to call humans in the position before the fall. This is God's original standard for humanity, and because that standard has been completely lost, we must break through this realm of death, and how miserable is God's position in having to do so? However, centered on the principle of creation, God is in the position of a parent who cannot consider dignity or face when searching for His children, so God's dignity has been trampled and diminished. 

In this way, God Himself has become like a beggar, being pushed around in the realm of satanic suffering, yet you must understand that He is in the position of a parent who is searching for lost children while enduring this. The pain of walking through the steps to find lost children is great, but... (The recording momentarily stops) God has endured this path of heartistic suffering until now.

It is not that He suffers from external suffering or external persecution. As He walks the path of conflicting resentments in His heart, He cannot express His grievances to anyone; if He laments, that becomes a condition for Satan to accuse Him, and if He complains, all the complaints become blessings and comfort before humanity, but rather remain as a path of resentment that Satan can accuse God of. Therefore, although He harbors a heart of resentment, He cannot express that resentment; although He harbors sorrow, He cannot express that sorrow; although He suffers, He cannot express that suffering; and although He feels wronged, He cannot express that injustice. You must understand that this is God's situation.

Why is that? Because the more He expresses those feelings, the more Satan rejoices. Satan accuses, saying, "From the perspective of the original principle of creation, you should be joyful toward humanity, yet you are in a position of sorrow, so you cannot find your children or love them."
Even if you suffer all kinds of pain in the midst of it, you cannot face humanity without having the connection of a heart that overcomes it and rejoices, can you? It is because of this original principle of creation that you cannot mourn even when you see your dead son, nor can you feel lonely when you see your lonely sons and daughters, can you? This is what is being accused. You must think about how difficult the path of internal suffering that God has been pioneering for the restoration process has been until now. God has sacrificed countless individuals before Satan while carrying out the history of restoration. Families have also been sacrificed, as well as nations and countries.

For example, Judaism and the nation of Israel sacrificed themselves by killing Jesus, and Christianity has been sacrificed for 2,000 years, but God cannot show a sad expression before Satan while holding onto these sacrificed groups, nor can He show resentment toward Satan. Even while witnessing countless groups being sacrificed, God cannot help but respond with an indifferent heart as if it has nothing to do with Him. You must understand that God is in a position of suffering that cannot be compared to any other pain. Standing in this position, God has come down through the historical process.

Jesus is truly the son of God who lived for God. History has come solely to pay the price to establish one person in this world. In other words, it had to endure suffering. During that period, God cannot come to earth freely. He cannot come as He pleases. Why? Because the entirety of this earth is occupied by the forces of darkness. To break through that, an infinite struggle must be fought. An infinite struggle must be fought to establish one person. That one person is the problem. It took 6,000 years for God to pave the way for that one person to come to this earth as the Messiah.

So who fights behind the scenes? God cannot fight directly. God is not supposed to fight with the archangel. It is not the principle for the master and servant to fight. So who must fight? The archangels must fight among themselves. Thus, until now, God has mobilized countless angels who follow His will and the spirits of those who have believed in God throughout history to pave the way for the ground on earth. He has made them walk the path of pioneering the earth.

On the peak of suffering. Today, there are many people living as they please, or claiming to follow the path of will, or seeking God with the intention of their own happiness, salvation, and fulfillment of their wishes. However, when they go to the spirit world, they will finally realize how much their lives have been in conflict with God's position and God's will. They are all in the position of receiving blessings because they serve God and being saved because they believe in Jesus. Many have sought the path of seeking God saying, 'God, please fight for me. Please take on the battles I must fight.' However, there has not been a single person in this world who has stepped forward saying, 'I will take responsibility for my battles and I will also take responsibility for God's battles.'

What is different about Jesus compared to the religious people who have come and gone throughout history? Other religious people are those who believe in their religion to receive blessings from heaven, but Jesus stood in a position where He wanted to comfort God by working for Him, rather than making God work for Him. This is what makes it different.

Throughout the historical process, many people have used God to receive blessings and hoped for comfort while leaving the burdensome work to God. This has been the path taken by religious people until now. However, the son of God, Jesus, understood how sorrowful God is, and therefore, He wanted to relieve God's burdens, not to ask God to relieve His own burdens. For this reason, in the historical process, He was finally able to say, 'Please entrust your burdens to me. I will take on your battles, and I will bear your emotional cross. God, if there are difficult things, please entrust them to me. God, if there are things you must sacrifice, let me sacrifice in your place.' You must understand that Jesus was the one who appeared as a son who could say this.

Because a son who could do this appeared in the historical process, God, who had been suppressing unspeakable emotions, was finally able to burst forth with a heart of weeping, saying, 'You alone understand my heart.' It was a weeping of gratitude, a weeping of fulfillment of wishes, and a weeping that represented the joy of reunion that welcomed Jesus Christ. This was possible because Jesus Christ chose the path of saying that He would live or die for the will and for God, and went the way of saying, 'Let your will be done.'

From a human perspective, no one desires the path of suffering. When Jesus faced the cross and prayed earnestly in the Garden of Gethsemane, He said, 'Abba, Father, take this cup away from me. Yet not what I will, but what you will.' (Mark 14:36) His position is different from that of others.

When we look at the purpose of creation, no one is destined to walk the path of suffering. Therefore, our human nature does not desire pain, and no one has the heart to gladly accept the path of suffering. However, because Jesus knew God's will, He stood in a heartfelt position to suppress His own desires of creation and take on God's suffering.

With the emergence of Jesus Christ as such a son, the foundation of happiness on this earth began to be established, and God's connection began to be formed on this earth.

We must follow the thoughts of Jesus. Although Jesus was just one man, His heart was filled with God's heart. Furthermore, Jesus' heart was not only filled with God's heart but was also in a position to feel God's heart. When Jesus fought against the enemies that had a connection to God's heart, He did not fight against personal enemies but stood in a position to take responsibility for the global and cosmic stage of Satan's dominion that remains in the universe.

Because God's position is such, Jesus stood in a position of a son fighting against the enemy, determined to conquer that global enemy, making Him someone God could trust. In other words, in enduring suffering, He took on God's pain, in taking responsibility, He took on the responsibilities that God should bear, and in fighting, He resolved to eliminate the Satan that remains in the world on behalf of God, thinking that if there is a possibility to achieve this through death, it is natural to choose the path of death. You must understand that this was the step taken by Jesus Christ.

When we think of this, today, each of us must follow the thoughts of Jesus. Those of us who stand in the position of the bride of Jesus must regard Him as our elder brother, as our father, and furthermore, as our bridegroom. Why must we do this? Because Eve lost three kinds of love all at once due to her fall: the love of a father, the love of an elder brother, and the love of a husband. Because Eve lost these three kinds of love while facing one man, Adam, she must restore these three kinds of love according to the principle of restoration through indemnity to be able to face her bridegroom. Therefore, it is the fate of fallen Eve that she must seek a Lord who can be loved as a father, as an elder brother, and as a bridegroom.

You will meet this bridegroom in the present age, but the historical starting point, background, and content with the bridegroom are all different. When a woman gets married, she must follow the duties of her husband's family and emulate the traditions of that family. She must also align herself with what her husband does, and furthermore, in her emotional life, she must always be a friend to her husband. The bride cannot be happy when the bridegroom is sad, and the bride cannot stand in a position of rest when the bridegroom is lonely. The bride cannot be happy when the bridegroom is miserable, and if the bridegroom is miserable, the bride is naturally miserable as well. If the bridegroom is happy, the bride is naturally happy. In other words, the bride's destiny is not determined by her own assertions or will, but rather by the bridegroom.

When we look at the bride, her success is determined by whether she welcomes the bridegroom well or not. No matter how excellent a woman may be, if she fails to welcome her bridegroom well, her excellence will not be revealed. The bride's destiny stands in the same position as her husband's destiny, so no matter how excellent the bride may be, she will follow her husband's destiny. If she deviates from her husband's destiny, she cannot be a bride. You must understand this.

Then, who is the one who can come to you as a bridegroom? He is the one who comes from the position of a father, and the one who comes from the position of an elder brother. He must be someone who is connected to me with perfect brotherly love, someone who cannot be denied by anyone, someone who is my brother, and even if the father who gave birth to me in this world denies it, he cannot be denied. Even if the blood relatives or elder brothers deny it, he cannot be denied. You must enter into a position where you cannot deny him.

Without having a connection to the heart world of the bridegroom, you cannot restore God's emotional standards. When you realize this, you cannot return without experiencing these three stages of love that seem like a bridegroom, seem like an elder brother, and seem like a father. What must be centered? It must not be centered around oneself, but centered around God.

You are not in that position simply because of the fall itself. To be in that position, first, the bridegroom's purpose must be clear. Because he is in the position of a bridegroom, his efforts are my efforts, and his destiny is my destiny. Only when you can feel the three kinds of love as a father, elder brother, and bridegroom within the absolute unified dominion can Adam and Eve be in the realm where they have not fallen, and from that higher position, you can restore the emotional connection of the starting point that Adam and Eve had before the fall. You must understand this fact.

Today, when we talk about True Parents, True Children, or True Couples in the Unification Church, you must recognize that these words are the gospel among gospels before humanity, more than anyone else's words that have come and gone throughout history. Think about how long it has taken for True Parents to appear. Humanity fell and came to this position, so we must rise to this level. In this position, one cannot become parents. When looking at the fallen realm, we must rise into the realm of growth.

To rise into the realm of growth, what must we do? We must fight against the realm of Satan and win from the position of growth. This position of growth is the position of the archangel. We must win from this archangelic position. To create the authority to win from the archangelic level, we cannot be in this position. We must occupy all of this. If there is an archangelic realm on the left side of Satan, we must create the archangelic realm on the heavenly side here. In other words, we must establish a foundation where the spirit world can freely ascend and descend centered on God.

From here, if the bride and bridegroom become one according to the principles, they can rise to this level. However, they cannot become the center. This becomes the foundation for the returning Lord to carry out the work of restoration. However, for the Lord to come to the earth, He must integrate the spirit world and achieve victory. Otherwise, He cannot come. Right? Only when the victory of the spirit world is established can He come to the earth.

After establishing the victory of the spirit world and coming to the earth, the people on the earth must absolutely become one with the spirit world. However, as the saying goes, "the hearts of people change like the morning and evening," people fluctuate and change in the morning and evening. If they change like that, what happens? Because of the invasion of Satan's realm, to rise, one must engage in a terrible struggle to occupy Satan's realm. Only after preparing countermeasures against that can one finally rise. This is the struggle we are engaged in.

Know that there is an increasingly intensified path of suffering as time goes on. Looking at you, the members of the Unification Church today, if the path of this will becomes better, it would be fine, but the truth is that as time goes on, there is an increasingly intensified path of suffering. Therefore, one may come to the point of saying they cannot go on. Think about it. Is it easier now than when you first started? It is not easier. Right? How difficult was individual restoration? It took 6,000 years. So how difficult do you think family restoration will be? Without being prepared to die, one cannot restore a family. You must understand this.

When looking at numerous religions, the emphasis on living a single life without recognizing marriage was to restore the standard of the archangel before the fall and the standard of Adam before the fall. This was to find one fallen Adam before the fall. In this way, if a counterpart is permitted here, what must that counterpart be? It must be absolute. There must be no fluctuation. Even if one must die, they must be able to say, "He is my lord," and even if they live, they must say, "He is my lord." From night to day, from youth to old age, there must be no other man or woman, and the thought must be that Adam is only for Eve, and Eve is only for Adam. When the family becomes one like this, it does not end here. After that, the tribe must be restored. Is that not so?

Restoring a family is more difficult than individual restoration. For a family to become one, what must be done? If that family is to be a family that serves two worlds, it must be divided in half. Shouldn't it be so? The left side must be cut off centered on the family. Centered on the tribe, there must be no left side. Only when there is no left side can one rise. Only then can one continue to rise.

Today, the members of the Unification Church are showing the most dangerous tendencies of ideological decay. In the 1960s, when you fought individually, you were willing to die, go hungry, or endure persecution without any problems, but now that you have received blessings, there is a tendency to want to settle down. Is it right to want to settle down? Wouldn't it be great if you could settle down? How earnest would God be in wanting that? However, if you settle down, you will perish. You will perish. If you settle down, you will perish. Is it possible to settle down or not? Therefore, family restoration is more difficult than individual restoration.

They must be a couple who can say, "You and I were born for this purpose, and we exist for this purpose; we cannot live without resolving this, nor can we die without resolving it." 

However, do you think you can live comfortably? If you live comfortably, who will restore the tribes, who will restore the nations, who will restore the countries, and who will restore the world? Who will do it? You might say, "God will do it," but because humanity has fallen, it must be done through humanity; thus, humans must take responsibility. Who must take responsibility? Adam must take responsibility because he caused this situation. Even if I bear the sorrow of the heavens and the earth, I must take on that responsibility. God should not do it. Who must do it? Adam must do it. A couple standing in Adam's position must be a blessed family! But can you just settle down? When you have children, you must think of them as children who need to be carried instead of just being a burden.

We have no nation and no place to settle. We have not inherited the decisive foundation of rest from heaven to the earth. This is the path of filial piety that our children must follow.

The Path We Must Take

The people living on this earth are walking through the journey of life day by day. When looking at each individual, when you wake up in the morning and carry out the tasks you are responsible for that day, there is a path you must take. If there is no direction set for how you will fulfill your responsibilities and how you will spend your day, then everything you do that day will yield meaningless results in front of any purpose or intention you may have for the future.

Purpose and direction must be the same.

Therefore, if someone is to embark on a path, that person must first set a principled direction they must go, and by fulfilling some purpose that can add to themselves, they will envision a more advanced self than their current self. This is the way humans always wish to live.

That is why a direction must be established. The direction is the issue. That direction must align with the purpose you are pursuing. If the direction is set incorrectly, the purpose will also be wrong. If the direction you set this morning is different from the direction you set yesterday morning, then today will yield a different result than yesterday. In other words, when the direction I think today is different from yesterday, all the efforts I made today will have no relation to yesterday.

When looking at a year, if you move for a year based on a certain direction you set, and then the following year you move in a different direction, that new direction will have no relation to the past year. Even when looking at ten years, if you have walked with a certain direction for ten years, but after ten years you take a different direction, this will yield results that have no relation to the past ten years.

Now, when looking at an individual’s life, if there is a person who has made efforts every day in the same direction throughout their life, that person will ultimately reach a single result through their life’s achievements and contributions. When that single result ends with that person, it becomes a result for themselves alone, but when that result becomes for many people, for all humanity, then it becomes a result that represents the whole.

If this is true for an individual’s life, it must also be true for history. Although the ancestors of humanity fell, if we look at history from the fall to the present, if the direction humanity has pursued for a thousand years differs from the direction pursued from one thousand to two thousand years, the world would have encountered a different result. Or if the direction changed from three thousand to four thousand years, or from four thousand to five thousand years, then the position of the purpose would also have brought different results in various directions.

When we think about this, if God exists, what would He do? If God exists, what direction would He take?
