To become a virtuous woman

When we say "the country of etiquette," do you think it refers to "the eastern etiquette of men" or "the eastern etiquette of women"? When we refer to Korea as the country of etiquette, does it seem to refer to men or women? "Women." It seems to refer to women, right? "Yes." Let’s agree on that without arguing. Even though I am a man, I will side with the women. (Laughter) The term "the country of eastern etiquette" refers to women. Therefore, it concludes that the women who truly wanted to serve their husbands in the historical process of Korea were those who could not freely manage their households.

You should trace the history related to virtuous women and the monuments of virtuous women. If she is a daughter-in-law, she is a daughter-in-law who wakes up at dawn to prepare breakfast, and even when eating, she waits with water ready by the stove, fearing that her in-laws might ask for water. She does not eat thoughtlessly but eats with her heart always prepared, thinking, "Will my in-laws say, 'Hey, dear, bring me some water'?" A woman who lived such a life cannot become a virtuous woman.

Moreover, a virtuous woman is not a wife who lives freely centered around her husband. Are monuments for virtuous women established for women who have treated their husbands well or for those who have served their parents well? "For women who have treated their husbands well." The husband? Then does that mean it is okay for the in-laws to cry as long as she cares for her husband? "No." A virtuous woman cannot exist without being a dutiful daughter-in-law. She must first become a dutiful daughter-in-law.

To become a virtuous woman, what must she first be? "A dutiful daughter-in-law." She must first become a dutiful daughter-in-law and then become a virtuous woman. Therefore, the tradition of virtuous women is to think of parents first, not husbands. By thinking of parents in such a way, she receives the title of dutiful daughter-in-law, and even after that, when her parents say, "Now don't just take care of me, take care of your husband too. I am fine with whatever you do. That is enough," even after receiving such consent, if she turns around and thinks, "Oh, how nice! My time has come. I have been waiting for this time," (Laughter) such a woman can never become a virtuous woman.

If her in-laws say, "Dear, how can this girl not care for her parents more than for her husband? I want to care for my parents until I die and even after I die, so please do not do that," she must say that. If her in-laws still say, "Okay, that's enough. You can stop now," she must be a dutiful daughter-in-law who backs away while shedding tears and choking up, or she can never become a virtuous woman.

However, when she is in her husband's arms, if she says, "Oh, to hell with my in-laws, I want to go alone," that does not make sense. She must have a heart filled with gratitude toward her in-laws, who lovingly gave birth to her husband, saying, "How much love did my parents give to raise my husband? I will love him more than that love." She must have the heart to embrace her husband instead of her in-laws. Shouldn't it be like that?

Then, when her mother-in-law says that she does not need to be dutiful anymore...
just as I heard it from my husband when he said, "You don't have to put that much effort into me anymore." I shed tears and vowed, "Even if I die, I will die for you. Isn't that the path a woman should take?" Without standing in an environment where we can comfort each other and express gratitude, it is impossible to become a virtuous woman. 

We must clearly understand that this is the traditional position of a virtuous woman, right? "We must understand." If I say "all," then you must also say "all." We must understand, right? Where does love begin to resonate? It starts from the mother's womb; first, we receive the mother's love. The one who first loves in a relative sense centered around the child is the mother. The father loves too, but during the ten months when the child is in the womb, the mother cherishes and protects the child with a loving heart, being careful with her words, her actions, and her demeanor, going through the period of prenatal education. The person who loves the baby in the womb more than her own life is the mother. Love begins with the mother. Isn't that right?

By doing so, you must establish a tradition that can move the Unification Church members and the men. You need to understand all these facts.

Parents as the center of the family
In your family, you must honor the parents who are the center of the family. (While writing on the board) The same goes for the tribe; you must honor the parents who are the center. Everything must unite centered on the parents. It should not be centered on oneself but should all unite centered on the parents. Do you understand? The world must also unite centered on the parents. Therefore, you must act as a mediator to unite centered on the parents.

So, what is the tradition of the True Parents? Without this, history cannot be established, Satan cannot be separated, and the origin of a new historical tradition cannot be established. That is why this must always be a unified ideology within your realm of life, social realm, national realm, and world realm, creating feelings that can be called our home and our brothers, transcending nations, regions, and even borders, covering from one end of the earth to the other; that world is heaven. Do you understand?

You must love three nations. Looking longitudinally, there is the past, present, and future, and there are the three eras: the era of Adam, the era of Jesus, and the era of the Second Coming. Also, because three brothers have divided into three nations and expanded into a global nation, we must unite centered on those three nations. Therefore, to become a people who can live in the heavenly kingdom, that is, the world of heaven, you must love the peoples of the three nations.

In the future, you must understand that in Unification Church families, it is essential that someone marries a foreigner. Your descendants must marry a foreigner, one from the East and one from the West. That time is coming. Do you understand? “Yes.”

What is the path we must take? That path is always to push forward the family of the True Parents. You need to ride on that. Do you understand? You must follow the path that the True Parents walked. The family must go that way, the tribe must go that way, and the nation must go that way. When the nation is restored, it will be when such a lifestyle system becomes harmonious throughout the entire nation. And when that becomes harmonious globally, the world will be restored.

Therefore, centered on God, you must unite with the parents, and then? With the children, right? You must become one with the children. That is why even when you go to America, you must unite with the parents centered on God, and then you must unite with the children. Even when you go to Germany, you must unite with the parents centered on God and unite with the children. Looking at this longitudinally, the first position is God's position, the second position is the parents' position, and the third position is your position.

Also, looking at this laterally, the parents become the central point. Therefore, you must unite centered on the parents, and then you must unite centered on the parents' sons and daughters. Looking laterally, isn’t that the case? Then, you must unite. Considering this point, there is no place to connect without centering on the teacher’s family. Do you understand now?

The origin of the establishment of heaven
So, what kind of family is the family of the True Parents? The family of the True Parents is a historical passion, a center of the times, and a future origin. Therefore, when the world we live in becomes the hopeful heaven in the future, the homeland of tradition will be the entire life that the True Parents lived. Do you understand? When you ask what the ideological basis of the nation is, this is that ideological basis. And when you ask what the origin that can establish the world is, this is the origin that can establish the world. Do you understand? You must always form the three generations centered on the relationship of being children of the True Parents. God, parents, and you, that is the three generations, right? Looking laterally, it is the teacher, the teacher’s children, and then you, that is the three generations. You must understand that if you do not complete this three-generational realm, heaven and earth will not unite.

That is why you must serve the parents for more than three years. Serving the parents for more than three years must be done by the family, and then the nation must serve them, and the world must serve them. That is indeed how it should be. That is how you will reach the realm of world restoration. Looking at the number three, it means that you must serve for more than three years. Therefore, for three years, you must live together with the parents, eating together, discussing together, and living together. Your home must be like that. You must live as a peaceful and happy family that speaks only good words and lives joyfully for a period of three years.

If you live like that, even if the couple has a reason to fight, they cannot fight. Even if they want to fight, they should first ask the parents and then go into the room to pray. When praying, the wife should cry and say, “My husband has this kind of heart, and I have this kind of heart.” The husband should also pray, saying, “I have this kind of heart, but my wife has this kind of heart. Should I fight with my wife or not?” Then the answer will be, “Do not fight.” (Laughter) If there is a reason to fight, you should say, “Honey, let’s pray.” That is how it should be.

And when the husband goes out and returns, he should always prepare to give what he brings home to the parents first. You should live as if you are truly serving them. Are you doing that? You must prepare meals for the parents at breakfast, lunch, and dinner. You must do it well. And what will you do with that? You must be ready to host precious guests whenever they come. You should be waiting, thinking, “I hope someone comes from the headquarters; it would be nice if the teacher comes, but if the teacher doesn’t come, maybe the district leader will come, or perhaps someone from the headquarters will come.” If there is a family that is waiting all day with such sincerity, that family is a heavenly family. God cannot help but bless such a family. They wait with clothes prepared and food ready…

Then, what happens when that becomes a nation? It means that when the nation prepares a banquet to host the Lord, that time will come. Every day, they will set the banquet table and think, “Oh, I wonder if the Lord will come? I wonder if a precious guest will come from the headquarters? I wonder if someone from above will come?” They will have the heart to wait for a thousand years and wait for three hundred sixty-five days as if each day is the same, preparing for that banquet. Do you understand? That time is coming.

Would you like to see that time come, or not? “I would like to see it.” In the future, there will come a time when we will only live by having banquets. It will not be long before there will be no eating except at banquets. This applies both to the nation and among the tribal leaders. There will come a time when they will compete and fight to take responsibility for serving the parents for three years. Do you understand?

Establishing the tradition of eternal heavenly life
However, the teacher cannot establish this tradition after he dies. In that way, the entire tribe must gather their sincerity to serve the parents, and through their efforts to do better than before, that tribe will not perish and will receive blessings in proportion to that. Isn’t that how it should be?

In dedicating to serve the parents, if you say, “Father, this year I must serve you better than last year. To do that, I must work harder and receive more of God’s love,” then it is only natural that God will bless you. You must try doing that. Then see if you will go hungry. You will not go hungry. Have you lived like that? Did you live like that or not? “I did not live like that.” You need to know more.

In the future, the nation will do this. Then, if there are twelve countries, or three countries, they will come together to do this. Then Asia will unite, and Europe will unite, preparing banquet tables to host the Lord on that joyful banquet day. How eagerly will they wait for that day when each Asian and each European can host the Lord with the things they have dedicated? There will be orchestras and famous people from all over the world gathering to celebrate that banquet day, preparing programs to wait for it… That is the future of heavenly life. Do you understand?
the earth are interconnected. In this sense, when we look at the current members of the Unification Church, it may seem grim and miserable, but truly... this is a fearful yet magnificent thing. Do you understand what I mean? Let those who have ears hear. (Laughter) Because of such things, those among you who will fall away will fall away in advance, and those who will not fall away will be subjected to trials repeatedly. Do you feel good or bad about this? Yet, if there are those who remain here, there will come a time when they can say, "I thought I had entered a small inn, but it turned out to be the inner chamber of a royal palace."

168   The Path We Must Take
Are you living like that in your neighborhood? Is your family living like that? In the future, neighborhoods will become like that. If you are the chief of the neighborhood, the people will gather around the chief's house every day, offering their sincerity, competing week by week to bring rice and food, and there will come a time when they will treat each other as guests. This will transcend villages, streets, and even countries, so that whenever guests come to our neighborhood, we will be prepared to host them. What else could be called a heavenly nation if not this? Isn't that right? This can only happen through the tradition of True Parents. Do you want to go to such a nation or not? Do you want to live like that or not? If you want to, then you must live like that. So, even when you dress, how much sincerity must you put into preparing yourself? Everything must be done with such sincerity. Especially for women, there are many things to consider, right? All of these must be taken into account. There are many laws like this.

Then, looking at the standards for living as a heavenly family, have you lived a life that has passed or failed until now? "I have lived a failed life." Yes, you have lived a failed life. From now on, you must follow my words. Do you understand? "Yes." Since you have started, you must go well until the end. Therefore, you must understand the issues regarding your husband, the church, and your household better in order to create a new tradition. If you cannot do this, you will not only leave behind a lifetime of regret but also will not be able to face your parents. You must live knowing this. Do you understand? "Yes."

Now is the time to make true sacrifices to leave behind a new tradition. The time when the parents can rest is not now. If we do not find the nation, we cannot rest. Do you understand? Our wish is unification. Even in our dreams, our wish is unification. We must not stop our steps toward finding that nation and must shorten the time as we go. If we do not find it in our youth and reach our old age, it will be a regret. Therefore, we must all pledge to break through this path that heaven desires as soon as possible, putting forth all our sincerity. That is why we are going out to fight for the nation. Do you understand? It is for the nation.

Even when you face a humble meal in a lacking position, you must shed tears unknowingly. If the life of a child serving their parents is a step taken to find the nation, how can it be that you cannot even offer a sincere meal to your parents and cannot create an environment where you can offer your sincerity? You must live in such a way that you can feel fear for your own unfilial behavior. 

Deep in your heart, amidst the cries that repeat hundreds of times, you must say, "Father, Mother, hello. In order to welcome the day of victory along with the will, to enjoy joy and glory while living with you, we must endure and go on, as it is our mission. This is a path we cannot take without going through such a process, so please accept this position willingly." You must live with tears and a constricted heart. This is the life you must lead now. Do you understand?

Then, will you live alone like this? No. What is the glory of God? The glory of God is not in having one son alone, but in having two. Even if there is a daughter, having two is more glorious than having one. The more people you have under your care, the more glory there is in that household, isn't it?

What is the glory of parents? When they reach sixty, if they have many descendants and those descendants can provide for their parents, that becomes joy, glory, and pride for the grandparents celebrating their sixtieth birthday, doesn't it? That is why, in order to prepare a foundation that can be a source of pride before God centered on oneself, one must think, "If night comes, let it come; if day comes, let it come. My wish is to leave behind many glorious children before God." 

Among the descendants of those who have put forth such sincerity, there will be governors who can rule a district, there will be governors who can take responsibility for a province, and there will be presidents who can govern a nation. Furthermore, due to that utmost sincerity, there will be sovereigns who can rule the world. When we think of this, parents who have many such descendants are blessed parents, aren't they?

The true parents of heaven must stand in a position where they can do this more than anyone else. That is why I am going out with the thought of making true sacrifices to leave behind such bloodline and true tradition. You must understand that now is the time for you to move with such thoughts. Do you understand? This applies to your husbands, your children, and your church as well...

Until now, the ideology of Unification Church members has not been sufficient. Therefore, all the ideologies of Unification Church members until now must be sent away. No one can enter the heavenly kingdom with such ideologies. Everything must be related to the parents, decided with the parents, discussed with the parents, and resolved with the parents. However, husbands with such a mindset have not existed, nor have you with such a mindset. The only path we must take today is this path.

Let us remember that we are pioneers in building the kingdom of heaven and overcome all difficulties.
This path is a historical fruit, a center of the times, and a traditional origin for the future. Therefore, even after a thousand years, without following this tradition, we cannot live in heaven or go to heaven. This tradition must be carefully inherited by our Unification Church today. We must walk this path as individuals, as families, as tribes, as nations, as countries, and as a world. You must know that this is the traditional path of the true parents that the members of the Unification Church must walk, and you must understand that you cannot live otherwise.

Do you understand? "Yes." Then, what if the teacher cannot do these things while alive and passes away? What will happen if the teacher is no longer in this world? Think about it. Will your children be able to inherit that tradition? If you live like this and something happens to the teacher, can you have that tradition or not? If that happens, you cannot establish a tradition centered on the nation, nor can you establish a tradition centered on the world. If you cannot establish this, the question of when heaven will be realized on this earth becomes a problem.

That is why you must be pioneers and builders who lay a new cornerstone in history and build a new structure on it. Even if your path is difficult, do not complain but digest it with a joyful heart, and I ask you once again to take responsibility for establishing the holy laws of heaven. I will conclude my words here. Do you understand? "Yes." Now, let those who are willing to do so raise their hands.

<Prayer> Beloved Father, we have come to know that what we have longed for in the path of historical indemnity is the family of True Parents. Upon welcoming the family of True Parents, we realize that it is not a smooth family. That family is a den of tears, a crossroads of misery, and a family in a position to indemnify sorrow. When we think about this, we must feel the sorrow of the middle and the intricacies of the circumstances, and we must realize that we must quickly fill this pit of sorrow by offering ourselves as a sacrifice centered on heavenly relationships. We, as members of the Unification Church, are well aware of this.

Among us, the blessed families must take responsibility for such trials and tribulations, yet we stand in a position where we have not fulfilled that responsibility despite having gone through ten years of history. Therefore, in the 1970s, in order to establish a tradition of families that can make the Father happy, we have brought forth the women here to the Korean Peninsula.

Father, we have reached a point where we must change the training course we have followed until now. Now, centered on today and tomorrow, we must arm ourselves with a new ideology that can counter communism. And we are in a position where we must depart on the 8th. Rather than lamenting our inability to return to our hometown, we must have the mindset of a woman going out to serve her nation, shedding tears as we look toward the nation, and we must truly recognize the holy grace that has allowed us to align our hearts with the nation.

When we think that the core path True Parents must take is to pass through the nation, the country, and subdue the sovereigns of the world, we must pledge to take responsibility for this work, even at the cost of all sacrifices, and become those who can fulfill the dignity of a daughter who can make the Father happy.

We have clearly understood that the path we must take is the path we must walk with True Parents. The path of True Parents is the path that aligns with historical direction, the center of the will of the times, and the origin of tradition for the future. Today, we have come to know that the glory of being able to carry the name of True Parents is something that cannot be exchanged for any amount of wealth.

Many nations have sacrificed to find True Parents and meet them, and many good people have paid the price of blood and disappeared from the pit of resentment. When we think about this, we must fulfill this responsibility as blessed daughters of heaven who must indemnify all of this from the historical summit.

They must prepare themselves as sincere offerings, dedicating their bodies and minds. We have understood that we must stand in a position where we can serve the owner, serve our parents, serve our children, and serve our husbands as living sacrifices, not dead ones. Therefore, we have started for this purpose, and at this time, we resolve to unite for this work and to fight for this work until the end. Father, please bless us.

Father, please protect the path we are to take in the future, and please protect the current position of the Republic of Korea. Since May of this year, we have entered into a prayer position.

In order to take away the power of the satanic world centered around Kim Il-sung's party in the North, we must unite powerfully with the heavenly world, and we have come to understand that we must be one with the center. Therefore, let each of us maintain the position that must be united with True Parents and let us practice this. I earnestly ask you to make us understand that this is the way to protect this nation and save the world.

Father, please manage the situation in Asia and establish a victorious heaven, and please manage all nations to establish your liberated heaven. I earnestly wish for this. For that, I ask you to open up all living environments with sincerity and to intensify the life of serving, so that we can fulfill your victory in a three-dimensional, longitudinal, and lateral way, and become your daughters who can be examples.

I place everything before you, so please allow us to remain with your will as we fight against Satan. I pray in the name of True Parents. Amen. 

4) 
Connections and Missions
After completing the training process over the past few days, you are now in a position where you must each go out to the places promised by God tomorrow. When you think about this, you may feel a mix of newness and excitement.

First, let us thank God for allowing us to safely conclude this gathering. Now, as we consider the significant mission entrusted to you, a mission that can only exist for a time, a national and global mission, I sincerely hope that God's blessings will be upon you as you face the path ahead as fragile women.

You must now go to the corners of the Korean Peninsula, seeking out towns that no one expects. You will be engaging with people day and night. Whether it be grandfathers, grandmothers, young women, or young men, the larger the town you encounter, the more diverse the faces you will meet. There will be round people and tall people, talented people and less talented people, educated people and uneducated people, city dwellers and rural residents. Among those living in rural areas, there will be people who struggle to eat three meals a day, who are starving and suffering.

On May 7, 1971 (Friday), at the Central Training Center. 
* This message was given at the completion ceremony of the Blessed Families Women’s Evangelism Team training, and it is published under the title "True Connections and Missions" in the 125th issue of the <Words> (published on June 15, 1971). 

175 
Various forms of people will appear before you, and although you may only meet and connect with them in a temporary environment, you must always remember that countless historical sorrows and grief have been intertwined until that meeting. No matter how unattractive or unfortunate a person may seem, no one can know whether that unfortunate person may become a turning point in your life.

Therefore, you should not disregard or look down on someone simply because they do not meet your expectations. Likewise, you should not overly welcome someone just because they are the person you were hoping to meet. Regardless of the historical connections that person may have, trusting or relying on them could lead to loss.

What I want to convey here is that there is a connection in everything in the world. That is why I want to speak briefly on the topic of "Connections and Missions."

Misguided Connections and Reality
Where there is heaven, there is earth. When we think about it, heaven and earth seem to be separate entities, but they are always connected. Heaven and earth have entirely different contents and forms, yet they are always bound together by an inseparable connection.

Furthermore, heaven and earth, and between them, humanity, are referred to as "Heaven, Earth, and Humanity." This means that humanity exists because there is both heaven and earth, and also because heaven and earth are interconnected.
To connect the earth, it means that a person is indispensable. 
In other words, it is through a person that we connect with heaven and through a person that we connect with the earth. 
When viewed from the perspective of a person, if we see the person as a whole, it becomes the world’s humanity; if we look at a smaller field, it becomes a nation; if we break it down further, it becomes a single tribe; if we break it down even more, it becomes a single family; and if we break it down further, it ultimately results in man and woman. Thus, these two people, man and woman, can represent humanity. 
There are men and women among people. Men and women differ in all aspects, including content, personality, and talent, but they maintain an interdependent relationship that cannot be severed. There is a standard of connection in people, and based on that connection, men and women are born, with men representing heaven and women representing the earth. In comparative terms, that is how it is. In other words, the father represents heaven, and the mother represents the earth. Because of such connections, the universe exists. Therefore, the absolute God and this created world are bound together by an inseparable relationship. 
Is there anyone who can sever that connection? There is no one who can sever that connection. There can also be no evil that can be severed. Furthermore, even God Himself cannot separate all that is connected to the created world. 
You must understand that without establishing connections in a normal position and without bringing about the results of purpose in a normal position, there is no way to resolve the grievances of wrongly connected relationships. 
In our Unification Church, it is said that humanity originally fell. The ancestors of humanity formed connections of injustice that God did not permit, resulting in a world born from those unjust connections. In other words, among men and women, it should have been the man who became the master, but instead, the woman took the leading role and pulled the man out. 
That connection was not a proper connection but a twisted connection. Because it started from that connection, the world is not standing within the realm of rightful connections but rather within the realm that produces the results of twisted connections. 
In other words, everything has not unfolded according to rightful order but has developed through paradoxical and twisted content, and because it is tangled in such a twisted environment, we are living as fallen beings who suffer in these unwanted connections, and we know that this is the human condition in this world. 
In other words, due to the unjust connections, we humans have become entangled, and the question is how to transform this reality into a new connection. Those who have hoped for this and have worked hard until now are those who have fought with their conscience, establishing connections between heaven and earth based on their conscience, seeking the path of virtue while representing the connections of heaven and earth. 
People who take on the mission to correct these twisted connections are those who walk the path of virtue and engage in religious life. 
When we acknowledge the fact that we have fallen today, if there is a Creator who looks upon this fallen world, it can be seen that “that Creator cannot be understood as the rightful Creator.” This is how it is perceived. Humans, who are in unjust connections or twisted relationships, cannot understand an absolute being who is in a rightful and principled position, no matter how much they look upon Him. 
Humans born from non-principled and non-relational positions have come to the conclusion that “God is dead” at the end of the human world, and this is all a result of non-relational connections. Therefore, we cannot understand the rightful God, who is in the position of the original connection. 
While it is, of course, impossible to understand God, you today have been born into connections with fallen parents, and when we look at our parents, we do not know what kind of parents we should meet based on the original connection. Because we are children born from unjust connections, we cannot know our parents, whom we should honor according to the original connection, even if we try our best. Moreover, when we look at our siblings, they have all been born according to unjust connections, so even if we try to contemplate the original connection of siblings among those who share that connection, we cannot know it. Although we are told to love one another as siblings, we have lived until now without knowing how to love in a true sibling connection. 
When we look at a family, that family has existed based on unjust connections, so when we view it from that family itself, we do not know what a family born according to the original true connection would be like. We are humans born from such unjust families, and these unjust families have come together to form unjust tribes, unjust nations, and nations and worlds based on unjust connections. 
No matter how much we think about those nations and tribes, we cannot know what a tribe based on the original connection is like, what that nation is like, or what that country is like. 
Countless people of the world are now all pursuing one world, but they do not know what the content of that original one world will be. Humanity that exists in a world woven together by unjust connections cannot know the world that will be formed according to the original connection. In other words, from the beginning to the end, we do not have connections that can be welcomed; rather, we possess connections that must be denied and cannot be accepted, and the fact that we stand in a realm of fate that must go against such paradoxical paths is miserable, and we know that this is the result of the fall. 
The love connection that a person should originally establish 
So where should I, this person, begin to correct the thread of connection? This is the question. When we look at this issue, the original connection must have been established from an absolute being, and if God exists, it must have been from that God. Without connection, it is impossible to establish a relationship or lay the groundwork for existence. Therefore, as long as there is existence, when we seek the subject that can be the motive for existence, that subject undoubtedly leads to God. In other words, God exists. Thus, the connection is established from God, heaven and earth arise from God, and humanity arises from God. 
Then who is God? If God is the owner of love, He possesses the highest love. Therefore, centered on that love, we humans must establish a relationship with Him. That love connection must exist between God and humanity. 
What is that? If we search and seek for the connection that can be brought from the highest God, what is the final conclusion? God is the Father, so there is no position for us humans other than that of children. There is no position beyond that either. From this perspective, the decisive standard that God is our parent is established. 
When we love, true love cannot exist without the relationship of father and son. The position where a father can love a son is one where he cannot help but love, even if it means sacrificing his life. Isn’t this the relationship between father and son? If such a love connection could be established, humanity would not have been unhappy. 
Today, even if one becomes the son of the President of the Republic of Korea, he can boast that he is happy among thirty million people, and no one can accuse him. How much more so if he were born as a son or daughter of the Creator who created heaven and earth, and if he stands in a position where he follows the natural and rightful connections without contradictions and conflicts, how happy would he be? Until now, we have not clearly understood this. 
If such sons and daughters exist, when they go east, their father would want to follow them east, and if the sons and daughters go together, the father would want to follow them together. If the father goes east, the sons and daughters would want to follow him east, and if the father goes together, the sons and daughters would want to follow him together. They go together, come together, live together, and even work together, so that connection is not a temporary connection but an eternal connection. 
Therefore, when something good happens, people say, “Oh, how wonderful! I wish it could be like this forever.” They do not wish for it to be so only for a time; they wish for the place of true love to be eternal. Thus, true connections do not change temporarily as they go along. You must understand this. Connections that are not true change at some point along the way. 
Love is eternal 
When aligning the circumference of a large circle and a small circle, it can be matched to a certain extent, but beyond that, they will separate. To a certain extent, there is a connection that allows for alignment, but eventually, they will separate. However, when it comes to completely uniting, there is no separation anywhere. 
Is there anyone who, after occupying the position of the highest love, wants to separate after living for about ten years? Is there anyone who wants to separate after living for about a hundred years? Forever, forever, forever…. 
What is it that wishes not to separate even if it goes on forever? It is in that place where they become one centered on love. Why do we wish to be one forever? Because two values can harmonize into one. When something has completely become one, it cannot be separated. It has completely become one. 
There must be a connection for humans to be completely united with the eternal Creator, but until now, we humans have not known that. If a man who can become one with such a woman exists, and if they have completely become one, that is, if they have become one based on God’s love, would that couple want to separate? They would not want to separate. They would want to live together forever. Of course, they want to live forever with God, but if they are a couple formed based on the original connection, would they want to live for a while and then stop? They would want to live forever, forever. 
Everything that exists within that realm of love, such as life or objects within that realm of love, or everything that exists within that realm of love, they would want to remain as they are forever. Isn’t that right? Even if the clothes worn by a loved one become rags, they do not want to kick them aside. Isn’t that true? 
When they completely become one, men and women unite centered on God, men unite with men, women unite with women, and then if couples completely unite, none of them would want to separate. When they completely unite, the hair of the groom belongs to the bride, and the hair of the bride belongs to the groom. That is how it is. Even if a hair of a loved one falls, they do not want to give it away saying, “This is theirs,” but rather they do not want to trample it underfoot. When viewed from that perspective, they want to keep everything of the loved one forever. 
Then how long would they want to keep the life of a loved one? Would they want to keep it for about a hundred years, or forever? Forever. They would want to keep it forever. If that is the case for humans, what about God? God is the same. If God has sons and daughters, He would not want them to live for about a hundred years and then die; He would want to live together forever, to be together, to work together, and to place them in a position where they can see each other. 
From this perspective, in a place where they can become one centered on love, they will all desire eternal life. Only in the world of love is eternal life needed; in other worlds, eternal life is not needed. Do you understand? 
True connection 
Then what should true connection be? It should be the great love connection of God, who is the center of all hope in the universe, the source of all life, the foundation of power, and the driving force of development. What kind of connection would that be? It is the great love connection of God, who created heaven and earth. If we hold onto that connection and become one with it, that is, if everything becomes one with God, then everything that is dependent on that connection can become ours. That is how it works. 
That is why it is said that “God is love.” This does not mean that God equals love. Right? When it is said that God is love, it means that God must have love in order to fulfill His role as God. If God has no love, He cannot fulfill His role as God. No matter how great a father is, if his heart is cold as a rock and as cold as a winter stone, can he fulfill his role as a father? If a mother is such a person, can she fulfill her role as a mother? It is the same.

The same applies to individuals as it does to families. For a family to move from a place of unhappiness to a place of happiness, it may be sufficient for the father responsible for that family to make efforts alone, but if the entire family, including the mother and children, works together, the conditions and contents of happiness can be brought about more quickly. 

If one person makes efforts, the foundation of happiness for that family can be established more quickly if the whole family works together. The happiness achieved by many people working together can endure over a long time compared to the happiness achieved by one person's efforts. The Need for a New Value System

What is needed here is not to say that God is dead, but rather that a new movement must arise that can resurrect the God who was dead, a God who can be welcomed back after being expelled from the historical era. It must inevitably arise. If there are people, there are human wills. If there are people, there are human desires. We have come to the end of the world centered on those desires. If there is a God, what is God's desire? Then, if there is a God who can manage the present world, what would be the method by which that God can manage the present world? It is not to assimilate with this world. Because this world cannot be a world that can please God, we must overcome it from a position of opposition. Only by enduring and overcoming can we seek a new path.

Then, what should we endure and persevere with? We must seek a new value system and center on that. We must seek new values regarding the world, new values regarding humanity, new values regarding ideology, or new values regarding love. When that value system begins with content that can align with God's will, that value system is fundamentally different from a value system centered on humanity. There is a significant difference. That value system should not be in a position separate from reality, but should establish a relationship within the realm of wicked reality to bring about a happiness that is superior to any happiness of the wicked world. Without discovering such an ideology, we cannot establish a standard for patience and overcoming, that is, for enduring and persevering. Therefore, the world is groaning at the point where it must negate reality and discover a higher-dimensional value system. Existential philosophy also arose from that perspective. To overcome reality, we must present an internal value system that can overcome reality. That value system cannot be formed by humans. No matter how much humans try, it will not work. It is already proven and remains in a realm that has entered. What is important here is a transcendent value, a higher-dimensional value. The content must not be vague. It cannot be based on the idea that "it happened like this in the past, so it will happen like this in the future." It must have practical content that can overcome and break through the conditions of the environment centered on our emotional experience in real life. The question is how to internalize that.

What does the Unification Church desire? It does not wish to assimilate with the world; it does not seek to align with the path the world is taking. If this path started in Busan, it must not stop in Busan. It must expand and return around the world. If it starts in Korea, it must not just return to Asia. It must go around the whole world and return. 
Korea, as the subject country, must fulfill its responsibility 
Who will do this? Centered on Korea, the subject country, it is my wish to have this done. If you do not want to do this, Korea will perish. This country will not become a leading nation, but a following nation. It will become a nation of servants. Will you become servants? You must shed this pitiful state of relying on others and live as masters. You must become a nation that can rise to the world of peace with the dignified rights that the sovereigns of the country exercised hundreds of times over. To do that, you must know that you cannot overcome from end to end. 
Since it started in Korea, it must end in Korea. Since it started in Korea, Korea must become the locomotive that travels around the world and lays down the tracks. In doing this, can Korea become the worst of the worst, a cripple? Absolutely not. This is not my ideology. Can we say that Korea, which has become unable to do that in the world, is the best just because it started in Korea? Just because it did something first does not mean it is the best. 
The heads of departments and district heads must understand how the Japanese evaluate them. A certain head might say, "I got 80 points or whatever," and calculate everything, but among those heads, they know who is who. No matter how much those heads boast, they do not even flinch. Even if they think their complaints are being heard, those people are thinking, "This guy..." It is the foolish child who brings shame to the family. Do you understand? You must understand this. 
If Korea is the subject country, can it be the subject country without me? When I go to America, I will not come back even if you call me to Korea. When I go to America, America becomes the subject country. Do not say anything about Korea. You must do what they cannot do. 
So what should you do in the future? You must make patience and overcoming the essence of your life and character as you go through global trials and tribulations. When this path starts here and returns to the original place, the path will become a solid road, making the world convenient and beneficial. At that time, a historical event will unfold where this will be eternally praised and worshipped. That is also the will of Heaven. It cannot be achieved by sitting idly. 
You must see this and know the future. You can know what will happen to you, what will happen to Korea, and how you are progressing towards the will by looking at your own attitude of faith, lifestyle, and attitude towards the will. By observing this, you can know where the conclusion point for your descendants will be. And do not boast about Korea. Until this time, I have fought and won based on the conditions of the environment, so perhaps that can be boasted about, but when this country does not unite with that and goes against it, this country and its people can become miserable. 
If you do not overcome, there will be no victory 
Now is such a time. Imagine if the Unification Church were to disappear. Imagine a society without the Unification Church. Will you be able to root out corruption in the future? That is what you must entrust to me. I will clean it up. The leaders of the ruling and opposition parties will come to me for training and will do as I say. I will do it in a year and a half. Just see if it can be done or not. We will equip you with ideological training. We will also provide ideological training for the military, so entrust it to us. Now the time has come to say such things. I am openly saying this in public because it has become a foundation that can be recognized by all. In the future, we will educate you and then bring you in. 
So by 1974, we are preparing to establish our own newspaper company. All the women at the headquarters will go out and sell newspapers. We must overcome the Dong-A Ilbo. That is why I am preparing to establish a newspaper company even if it means going into debt. I have the conviction that I will never lose as long as I promote it. To do that, you must work hard. After working hard, it will not lead to failure, but to a time when you can dance in harmony. 
However, no matter how much you dance in the east, dance in the west, dance in the south, or dance in the north, you cannot do so without dancing in the center. Dancing in the east, west, south, and north is for the time when you can dance in the center. You must not think that dancing in the east means you are dancing in the center. You must go to the center and dance to finish. 
For Korea, the subject country, to inherit the authority and pride of Heaven, you must endure and overcome more than any other nation or people in the world. There will be personal trials, family trials, tribal trials, and national trials. 
From that perspective, looking at the current situation, the Unification Church is in a state of emergency facing tribal trials. This is not an emergency for Reverend Moon, but an emergency for you. You must know that such a crisis exists. You must overcome it. 
Will the teacher always be in Korea? The teacher does not intend to live in Korea forever. Even this time, there are three purposes for going to America, but I am not talking about them. When you hear about global events reported in the newspapers or news from the outer world, we must understand how we should resolve in the opposite direction. To overcome opposition, there must be opposition greater than the opposition. Otherwise, it cannot be overcome. Victory cannot be achieved. This is a fundamental principle. 
Even if you are in Korea, you must keep your eyes on the world. You are already on the path you desire. You must run vigorously using that path. 
You must pave the way for yourself, whether you are a subject of the Unification Church, a beloved son before Heaven, or a loyal servant. You must go beyond the established foundation of the Unification Church and utilize that path one hundred percent so that your righteous foundation and that path can remain extended. When you think of this, you must overcome even better. 
Now, our entire family must mobilize to protect the 38th parallel, and we must become a family that can look towards the five northern provinces for the sake of the will and pledge for tomorrow's success. If it is such a family, it will not perish at this time. No matter how difficult it is, it will not perish. I believe that those who go forward with this will have victory, glory, and praise forever.

We did not realize that this path is the traditional way of those who walk in faith. We have been told to endure and overcome. I must overcome myself. I must endure and overcome. I must realize once again that we must become those who gather here, shedding blood and tears, to bring forth a family that can do so. We must be aware that we are the gathered people of unification.

Those who cannot realize their shame after speaking, and cannot recognize the absurdity after looking, cannot endure and overcome. When a greater nation and a greater multitude appear, you know that you will embrace them and weep. Now, we must become heroes who run the path of suffering more than anyone else and determine the final victory more than anyone else.

When we look at the current situation of Korea and the world, which is in a state of trial, we must realize that standing at the forefront, shedding tears of sincerity on your behalf, can be the motivation for you in all things and can leave your tomorrow.

Father, how urgent is the historical mission to connect Korea, Japan, and Taiwan? Now we must make a new determination. To the young hearts gathered here, where is the young blood that pulses through the hearts of the youth directed? Please let us feel that we must die in the place where we break through the enemy's trenches. This pulsing sound must move the world, move the history of the world, and restore the heart of the world. When we think that this is the mission of the Unification family and the mission of us who are centered around the headquarters within the Republic of Korea, even if no one else can do it, we must become a group that perseveres and overcomes, taking patience and overcoming as our life philosophy until the day we can face the Father.

We did not realize that there must be many such groups. At this time, the children who are prostrated before you must pledge to become those who can do so.

Father, you are a pitiful and lonely being. We know that there are no sons and daughters you desire on this earth, but we have resolved to become the remnants among this nation. This path is a lonely one, where even after winning, the whole world wishes to resent and hopes for destruction, a path without rejoicing. When we think about when there will be a day when we can rejoice with the nation and be welcomed by them, a day when all people can praise you, we come to realize that you are more pitiful and miserable than us. The children gathered here must know that today's misery is a source of pride, and tomorrow's misery is even more of a pride, and must carry the philosophy of patience and overcoming to stretch beyond the nation, beyond the state, to the world, and resolve to become your sons and daughters who will leave an unshakeable tradition and foundation.

We understand that the future path of Korea will determine the fate of Asia, so may our attitude of faith and sincerity align with your heart and the direction of your providence. We earnestly request and desire that we may prepare for a new decisive victory.

The most foolish group in Japan is the Unification Church group, and the most foolish group is the group that calls itself the Unified Alliance. Indeed. Until the time comes when this nation, Japan, and all of Asia unite to prepare a victorious Asia that can bring you joy, we resolve to advance and advance at this time, and we earnestly request and desire that you allow us to make this vow.

Today is a holy day, so may your love be with your children wherever they gather, and may this place not become a place of debt to those who gather here to pray with one heart towards this place, but may you repay them with the grace of love and glory. I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

When we think that all things have served as intermediary offerings closer to heaven than humans, we come to feel that humans stand in a position more shameful than all things.

Today, following this vertical relationship, we have mediated through the son, and from the position of mediating through the son, we have mediated through the parents, and by centering on the love of the parents, we have entered an era where we can see the horizontal beginning of history. When we realize that we must not reverse the order of this sequential process—from parents to children, and from children to all things—we come to feel once again how precious the created world you have made is.

May 24, 1971 (Monday), at the former headquarters church.

272   The Day of All Things and the Process of Restoration
Please accept the entirety of this day with satisfaction, and establish new promises and connections so that the spirit world may be welcomed from the earth and may be welcomed by all things.

<Words> As you all know, today is the '9th Day of All Things.' In terms of years, we established the Day of All Things on May 1, 1963, so this year marks the 8th year. 
Days like this, commemorated centered on our Unification Church, are festival days that no nation or people in the world possesses, and one of these festival days is the 'Day of All Things.' In our Unification Church, there are four major holidays: Parents' Day, Children's Day, Day of All Things, and God's Day. The Day of All Things is one of these four major holidays. Originally, there should have been God's Day first, followed by Parents' Day, Children's Day, and the Day of All Things, but it has been reversed, with Parents' Day, Children's Day, and the Day of All Things coming first, followed by God's Day. You may have a general understanding of why God's Day is placed later through the Principle. 
The history of the restoration providence is a history to find a family united with God. 
Due to the fall of the first human ancestors, Adam and Eve, at the completion stage of growth, the parents of humanity disappeared. In other words, true parents of humanity, whom God desires, should have been established, but that did not happen. God needed to have a family that could make Him happy, but such a family could not be established. Therefore, we know well that the vertical expectation centered on God could not be established. 
From that fallen family, fallen descendants were born. The fallen family has fallen into the realm of evil, unable to establish a relationship with God inside and out, and thus God has been working hard to find a family that can establish a relationship with Him. That is the history of the restoration providence. 
In seeking, we must find the family before the tribe, the tribe before the nation, and the nation before the world. And before establishing a family, we must first find one man and one woman. In other words, there must be one man and one woman who can naturally subjugate the center of evil, Satan, and command and direct him from a position that even Satan cannot deny. Without this, we cannot determine the position of God's sons and daughters. Only when such sons and daughters receive love from God can they become men and women who can represent God's love. Even if they become such men and women, there must be no resentment left between them. 
When viewed from the perspective of man and woman, the woman has become the cause of the man's fall, so the enemy of the man is the woman, and the enemy of the woman is the man. Adam, as a man, was in the position of the subject, and even though Eve, in the position of the object, may have tempted him with cunning actions, he had the responsibility to govern that. Nevertheless, by listening to the woman's words, he fell. From the perspective of such results, we must understand that the subject, Adam, who should have been in a position not to listen, ended up standing in the position of the enemy of Eve by listening to her. 
Even if one receives God's love, if it is received from a one-to-one position, the bond of true husband and wife is not established. A man and a woman appearing on this earth must not remain as two but must become one. A man is not a man for another man, and a woman is not a woman for another woman, but a man and a woman must become one centered on God's love, establishing a heartistic foundation that cannot be separated by anyone. This is the principled perspective on establishing the point of a true family. 
Before such a standard is established, the gap between God and humanity cannot be completely resolved. While there are issues regarding widening the gap between Satan and humanity, first, the gap between humans must be resolved. Then, standing in the position of a restored man and woman, we must resolve the gap with God that has arisen due to the sins committed by humanity throughout history. Without doing so, we cannot create a victorious realm of love, which is the principled perspective. 
What is the basis for establishing Parents' Day, Children's Day, and the Day of All Things? Parents' Day is established, Children's Day is established, and the Day of All Things is established, but who is at the center of these establishments? It is not centered on parents, nor on children, nor on all things. It is established centered on the love of parents. You must understand that no matter how much one becomes a parent, one cannot enter the position of true parents without establishing a bond of love that can unite with God, and children and all things cannot enter their true positions without this. 
God created all things before creating humans. After creating all things, He created Adam and Eve. When Adam and Eve grew up and formed a family, God's love was finally able to settle among them. In other words, God's love comes last. God's love is established at the very end. Of course, there is a bond of love centered on a son or daughter individually, but that is ultimately vertical. The love received by a man, as an individual centered on God, is a vertical foundation but not a horizontal one. 
Then where does the horizontal foundation begin? It begins with the unity of the man and woman who have received love from a vertical position. The unity of man and woman serves not only to end the vertical position but also to initiate the ideal of horizontal love. In other words, without the establishment of a couple, one cannot form a connection in the horizontal world. 
Looking at the restoration providence up to now, there have been people who received God's love, and God sent His only son to establish a foundation for love, but they could not fulfill the will. What was the reason? It was not because they individually could not receive love, but because they could not establish a foundation of love in the family. Because this was not established, the motivation for the horizontal love of the world could not be initiated, and the will could not be fulfilled on this earth. We know this. 
The origin of this horizontal love, viewed from a providential perspective, is the path that Christianity has fought for over the past 2,000 years, and it is the hope of the day of the Second Coming that Christianity ultimately looks forward to. 
The day of the Second Coming is not fulfilled merely by the coming of God's son; there must also be a bride who can welcome the coming son. When the bride and groom are determined, they do not live apart from each other but are completely united, and through this bond, the connection of children is established, allowing for the establishment of a central form that can form a nation centered on God. 
No matter how great a saint or a person who understands God's will may be, if they cannot establish the bond of marriage, they cannot fulfill the will alone. Establishing a family foundation is the ideal of creation, the ideal of the restoration providence, and the historical hope that emerges through the providential age. Moreover, this is the ultimate purpose of religion that can completely settle historical sins, and you must understand that it is the foundation of hope where Jesus himself can dwell to achieve that purpose. 
Without this internal standard being established, Parents' Day cannot be set. Where did the fallen parents of today start? They started from the position that fell from the completion stage of growth into a state without principles. Therefore, to restore this, one must rise from the position of a servant to the position of a son, and through the connection with the son, ascend to the realm of completion. 
What is this realm of completion? It is the realm that has not fallen. In other words, it is the realm where the original Adam could freely relate to God without falling. However, to enter this realm of completion, one must receive grafting through a true son. 
What is the mission that Christianity has undertaken up to today? It has prepared a foundation where one can receive grafting from the true son on a global scale. When God's true son comes and says, "Let everyone receive grafting from me," if the entire world receives grafting at once, it will transition into the realm of completion. The Second Israel realm has been expanded globally to provide a foundation where grafting can be received at once. 
What does the Second Israel realm correspond to? It corresponds to the realm of the angelic world. Why does it correspond to the angelic world? Because Adam has not yet entered the realm of completion. Although the work was initiated centered on the archangel, God could not help but love the archangel in a comprehensive manner. In other words, the realm where the archangel could perform complete love has been the archangelic realm up to now. 
What kind of position is the realm where complete love could be performed? It is not a position that has achieved relative ideals but an individual position. The Jesus who is in the spirit world, as well as those who believed in him well, are in a personal position, just like the angelic world. Angels are solitary beings who do not establish relative connections. 
When we look at the Bible, when the Sadducees came to Jesus and asked about a woman who had seven husbands, "Whose wife will she be in the spirit world?" Jesus replied, "In the spirit world, there is no marrying or being given in marriage" (Luke 20:35), which was said because the time had not yet come. 
Then what is the spiritual salvation that Christianity speaks of today? It is the restoration from the fallen archangelic realm to the unfallen archangelic realm. Just as the archangel had the responsibility and mission to lead Adam and Eve to the realm of completion, all angels below the unfallen archangel must cooperate in establishing the standard of completion that Jesus should have established on earth, in other words, they are to inherit and carry out the mission of cooperating in the history of re-creation. 
For the mission of the archangel to be completed, a man and woman centered on God's love must appear and establish the realm of relative love, thereby resolving the motivations that caused the fall of the archangel world and restoring them. 
Without this restoration, in other words, without standing in the position of sons and daughters that the archangel can protect, Adam and Eve cannot appear as the completed Adam and Eve. 
What is the responsibility of the Lord who is to come? He must inherit the victory of the archangel and the victory that Jesus has achieved in the spirit world. He must stand in the position of the heart of the archangel and receive the love that the archangel received. He must unite with Jesus, who stood in a position where he could receive more love than the archangel.

316   Depth of Faith
We must also consider the question of whether we will take responsibility for this fight in place of others. 
We must bear greater sacrifices than our ancestors did. God has been carrying out the providence of restoration not only now but throughout history, paying the price of many sacrifices along the way. And the scope of those sacrifices was not limited to one part; it transcended nations and moved the world, paying the price of sacrifice in such environments. Even if we only look at the history of Christianity, from the family of Adam to Noah, Abraham, Moses, Zechariah, and Joseph, we see that they paid a tremendous price of sacrifice over a period of 4,000 years.
In order to inherit the historical connections of sacrifice, we must bear a heavier cross and greater sacrifices than the ancestors of the historical era. Without individuals who can do so, there can be no progress, and we cannot pursue future values. It is only natural that without a group determined to sacrifice even more greatly, we cannot advance the providence of this world. Therefore, we must recognize that God had to seek out a group willing to pursue greater sacrifices than in the past to carve out this battlefield.
Grandfather Noah fought for 120 years. When we consider the period of 120 years, it is neither 12 days nor 12 years. This long period of 120 years can be seen as a precious time that corresponds to an entire lifetime. For Noah, 120 years was not just a remaining period of life; it was a time in which he could offer the most valuable segment of his life.
During that period, Noah endured suffering and fought steadily for 120 years, demonstrating patience, sincerity, and faithfulness to God's command that no one can deny. How much effort and sacrifice must he have made to stand in that position?
There must have been persecution at home, opposition from the neighborhood, and relatives who denied and misunderstood him. In overcoming such circumstances, there must have been days when he felt not joy but rather sorrow. Those days of sorrow were also days of trial, where he had to endure increased struggles and trials daily to overcome them.
As time went on, the trials did not decrease; rather, the trials of the intensified environment must have confronted Noah even more. When we consider this issue, we can see that Noah was indeed one of those who could be remembered as a person on God's side, carrying out the providence of history.
The same can be said for Abraham. When he left his beloved hometown, he did not leave grandly. He did not proclaim to his neighbors and relatives, “I am going to carry a mission at a certain time to a certain place.” Instead, he left alone at night, hiding himself, in a lonely state that no one knew about. That lonely aspect was not just a part of Abraham himself; that lonely position aligned with God's lonely position. If he had not started with such a origin, he would have had no relationship with God.
That lonely position was the same as the lonely position God was in, and that serious position was the serious position God was in. Because he had the resolution and attitude to separate evil, eliminate evil, and decisively deal with evil, God could not help but establish Abraham as the central figure who could integrate the entirety of God's providential history over 2,000 years; we must understand that there was such an internal connection.
The same can be said when we focus on Moses. Moses was thought of as a person who entered the Egyptian palace as an Israelite, standing in a position loved as the son of Pharaoh's daughter, having received special privileges. However, although he was in a luxurious position, he thought in his heart that the luxurious palace of Pharaoh was not the foundation of his desires. The more luxurious the environment around him was, the more it was not an environment that brought him joy, but rather an environment that stimulated his sense of nationalism, and it was a foundation that could inspire the independence of his people and ignite patriotic feelings.
When the Israelites fought against the Egyptians, the fact that he killed an Egyptian was not a sudden event. In his heart, there was a hope that the Israelite nation could be liberated and live as a peaceful and independent nation. As Moses lived a luxurious life in Egypt, the more vast and grand that luxury and glory were, the more there was a patriotic feeling within him that wished to overcome, disregard, and eliminate it. That moment when he killed the Egyptian was a manifestation of that patriotism.
Was that act of killing the Egyptian a position that God disliked? No. When God saw the Israelite nation suffering under the Egyptian nation for hundreds of years, there were times when He wanted to strike them down immediately.
From this perspective, Moses represented the hidden heart of God, who always wished for such a person to appear, and because he had that emotional starting point as a representative of the patriotic Israelite nation, God could not help but bring about a new beginning for the historical nation through Moses.
The same can be said for John the Baptist. In that era, there were many who hoped for the Messiah to come. Many scribes and priests must have earnestly wished for the Messiah to come. Some may have prayed all night, and many may have devoted their lives to preparing for that day. Among that multitude, God must have sought someone who could live in a way that was close to the wish He desired and the path of the Son He was sending.
The Israelite nation, the Jews, or the scribes hoped for the Lord to come in glory, but they were not in a position to receive the Son who could come in glory. The positions of those who were hoping for that and God's position were worlds apart. It was inevitable that they would not appear in the same direction. When we consider that the path God could come to was not a glorious place but rather a miserable one, we can be sure that God would seek out those who could bear the mission of pioneering that miserable path. When we think about this, we realize that there was a significant difference between the perspective of the Israelite nation towards providence at the time John the Baptist appeared and the perspective of John the Baptist himself.
John the Baptist went out into the wilderness, living a lonely life eating locusts and wild honey. Whether it rained or the wind blew... even if he saw flowers, there was no one to relate to in that loneliness. The desolate environment of the wilderness was indeed a stimulating environment that could connect his deep inner feelings with God.
When loneliness seeped in and difficulties confronted him in that desolate environment, he did not regard that loneliness and difficulty as merely his own but was in a position to sympathize with God's loneliness and God's difficulties. He was not a person living in a peaceful and free environment, but rather John the Baptist was in a serious position, overcoming difficulties in a lonely place, paving the way for the day that God desired to come.
From this perspective, John the Baptist was in a position to be a representative of the times, more than anyone else of that era, any prophet, or any scribe, because he had the connections that could bring him closer to the path where God would come. Therefore, it is reasonable to view that God could not help but seek out John the Baptist.
If there is a heartfelt desire for the Messiah to come, that heartfelt desire is not to solve one's own happiness by receiving the Messiah but rather a prepared heart to receive the Messiah as a representative of the Israelite nation. Thus, he was undoubtedly a representative who could become a pride and establish a traditional inner connection in the national and historical era or the era of God's providence, and through this John the Baptist, God sought to continue the will of providence.

Let us suppose there are two sons in a position to throw a party for their parents' sixtieth birthday. The older brother says he will do it to the utmost. He plans to sell all the property his parents have accumulated throughout their lives, sell all his own property, and even go into debt several times his own property to throw a party. However, the younger brother says that their parents do not want such a grand sixtieth birthday party, that the money their parents earned was for their children, not for themselves, and that it would be filial to throw a party with about a third of their property.  
When the parents watch the older brother, who is foolishly willing to sell everything and go into debt, and the younger brother, who wants to keep some and do it more modestly, who do you think the parents will consider to be the more caring child? Even if it is a rough way to go into debt, the son who wants to throw a party and go bankrupt will be seen as more caring than the one who thinks about the future and wants to do it without conditions.
Who do you think is the son who cares more for his mother and father among the sons?
