<Prayer> Father, I have come to understand that the path of faith is not a path that can be walked like the affairs of the world. We did not realize how serious your position is, as you govern with the urgent focus of the heavens rising and falling based on the results of a moment's action. 
Father, you know well the path that the Unification Church must take. You also know well the path that this child, who is leading the Unification Church, must take. 
I have already known the path I must take and have set out. Many people have passed by on this path. I have observed many people and experienced many encounters, so I know what people are like, and how people from different countries are. I have seen that people from South Korea are like this, people from Japan are like that, and people from other foreign countries are like this. 
However, I have come to understand that a person of heaven must be unchanging, even more so than a person from South Korea, Japan, or any foreign country. When I think that a person of heaven must be someone who can stand before any nation in the world and say, "That is right," it cannot be that faith in the Unification Church is only seeking Japanese people or only relating to American people. 
We must pursue the Father himself and rely on the Father. In front of this path, we must have a faith attitude that has the content of motivation to pursue the Father, regardless of any nation, anyone from the past, anyone from the present, or anyone from the future, and we must leave behind acts of practice. 
That journey is one that must pay the price of tears and blood, the price of love's sacrifice, and it is a journey that must follow the global connections that transcend nations and peoples. We have come to understand this, but we did not realize how serious it is. 
This morning, centered on the words "the depth of faith," I must reflect once again on how deep a position I stand in. Have we truly had a heart that resonates with the words, to the point of staying up all night, saying, "I must not abandon all connections, this is the only way"? Standing in a deep and profound emotional place, have we ever revered the Father and expressed gratitude for the amazing words? As I reflect on the past and reaffirm my current position, I hope this time will prompt a new awareness as I discover my own inadequacies. 
To walk the heavenly path, we must go through the path of becoming a sacrificial offering. We must walk the path of personal sacrifice. Men must become sacrifices, and women must become sacrifices. Not only men and women but also their sons and daughters must become sacrifices. While it is certainly true that the sons and daughters must become sacrifices, the clans connected to those sons and daughters must also become sacrifices. After the clan has become a sacrifice, the nation must become a sacrifice, and after the nation has become a sacrifice, the state must become a sacrifice. When we think of the tremendous fact that without this, we cannot cross the mountains of a thousand miles, we realize that today, the members of the Unification Church have been in a very superficial position. We must realize how much we have been immersed in self-centered thoughts. 
When looking at the morning sunlight, we must meet a new morning where the light of hope and liberation shines in this country, and when night comes, we must greet it with the heart that this night should not become a night that leaves conditions for Satan's invasion and accusations. In the morning, there should be gratitude, and in the evening, we must discover that we are in a state of lamentation, unable to have an environment where we can live in harmony with the Father. We must know that we must strive to eliminate such an environment. 
348   The Depth of Faith 
The visible universe has a free appearance that can sing of peace and happiness. We must realize that we are today’s believers who must lament for not being able to stand in the position of embracing and loving all creation, holding our sons and daughters who stand in the position of our desires. 
Since the world has already become evil, we must not have any lingering attachments to this world. We must know that we are those who must overcome this evil world and, to walk the path of faith, we must put forth all our efforts. 
When there is a path of suffering in front of us, we must not turn back but must go straight ahead, facing and enduring the challenges. Who would want to walk the path of suffering? But because we long for your love, we must walk that path, and because we long for your nation, we must walk the path of death. This is a step prepared to overcome the heaps of corpses that have been piled up, and as we think of the fact that that day has not yet come, we must offer our tears of gratitude to the Father and strive to present tomorrow as an offering before the Father, realizing that we are the descendants of a fallen lineage who have not understood this. 
We must tighten our collars and pursue the nation you desire, vowing to offer everything to the Father without leaving a path of life before the path of death. We must not just promise to walk this path once or twice, but we must commit ourselves to walk it every day, dedicating our lives. Yet, when we stand before the Father, who has overcome the path of suffering for 6,000 years, we feel that we are too inadequate and too unworthy. Every time we feel this, we find ourselves demanding curses before the Father after having given our all in love, and we know that our destiny is the fate of the fallen. 
In the course of such acts of faith, whenever we feel that there is no one we can rely on, we understand how lonely the Father was, and we know how sorrowful the Father was when he could not have the conditions to be opposed by anyone. We wish to become sons and daughters who can strive to be the counterpart to the lonely Father, and we sincerely hope to become those who practice such a unified faith. 
Father, this place where we bow our heads must not become a place that enhances your sorrow. We must become a gathering that can be swept away by the waves of love flowing from your heart, a place that can be occupied by your love. This altar must not become a place where the sound of weeping for your love ceases. It must be a holy place where we can meet your sons and daughters who are buried in your love, praising you countless times and striving to overcome the path of suffering. 
Here, this floor must be a place where those who wish to walk the pure path of the Unification Church must shed tears and sweat that have not yet been shed. We must become a group that can strive to shed tears and blood here. Although this place may be humble and may seem like a place of despair to some, we must recognize that through this place, the historical stories and grievances that no one in history remembers have been gathered, and the foundation of heavenly life has been established. 
When we think of this as the one place that cannot be absent in front of the wishes of a thousand years and the heart of your grievance, we must connect with the joy of being able to praise this place as a grateful and thankful place. We must realize that the Father’s grievance can be resolved from here, and we must not forget that we must become a group that can discover the amazing and holy self that has participated in this place. 
Father, even if we walk the path of the final destiny with a smile of joy before your coming footsteps, we must leave a connection that allows you to remember us all as your sons and daughters with a smile. We know that this Unification Church must be such a church. 
Father! Please remember your children here. I know that you still love the child standing here. I understand that your comfort, which no one knows during lonely times, still remains behind this altar. When we think of the many who worry about being presented before a world you do not desire, I know that you are surely with this Unification Church. Please remember your children who are bowed down here and nurture them well. 
It is not the Unification Church that leads them, but they must pioneer the future of the Unification Church. Therefore, as God who is in a position to love each of these individuals more than the Unification Church, the more I think about it, the more I realize that God is a pitiful being. 
On this day, the path of suffering, on this day, the lonely journey, on this day, the pitiful position must continue to be walked, and as we continue to walk the remaining path, there are many who are surrounding you, overcoming difficulties, and saying, "Father! Please endure and overcome." We understand that it is the Father’s situation that desires to overcome. Please forgive us for not having stood in such a position in the past. As we once again feel the inadequacies and unfilial actions before the urgent situation, we ask that you allow us to become sons and daughters who are willing to abandon everything to align our hearts with the holiness of the Father and the results of the Father’s victory. 
Please remember the children scattered across the nation, Father. I do not wish for you to remember me. Please remember these children as you see the future of South Korea and the world you are seeking. I know that the tears and sweat they have shed will not be in vain. Even if countless people have passed by, I feel that if even one person is absent, I must take on this task myself, and you know this well. 
That is why the Unification Church cannot perish, the Unification Church must bear responsibility, and the Unification Church must fight and endure until the end. You, who alone leads the destiny of this Unification Church, are indeed a pitiful being, and the sons and daughters who face your will are also a pitiful group. We know very well that the end of the actions of this pitiful group must not be miserable before the Father, and we must have the confidence that our hearts will not perish, pledging to fulfill the duties of filial piety and loyalty. May this place become one that can be surrounded by your heart of compassion and mercy, and may it become our environment of faith. 
I earnestly ask and hope for this. 
I sincerely hope and desire that you will remember your children scattered across the world. May this last Sabbath of May be a time for them to reflect on how deeply the depth of faith has penetrated their bones and flesh, how much they have believed, how much they have acted, how much they have loved, and how desperately they have struggled to lay their bodies on the cross. Now, as June approaches, we must overcome June with strength. 
Please protect the destiny that this nation and this people must follow, Father. When we think of Kim Il-sung of North Korea targeting South Korea centered around the age of 60, we must offer even more sincerity based on the principle that he must not exceed his sixties, so that we can bear all responsibility for the future of this nation and people and become a group that fulfills our mission. I earnestly ask you, Father. 
Today, I again request that you be with the altar and the children of Unification scattered across the nation with deep heart, comfort, encouragement, guidance, and love. I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. *
